Edith

**Edith**, a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)"), is an employee of [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf") and works in the depths of [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

She is incredibly dedicated to her mining duties and can be found hacking away 24 hours a day, without ever eating or sleeping.

She wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#0006ff43 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"), and is equipped with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). She carries a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When approached she can say:

:   *"Here to mine?"*
:   *"[Quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore") is rare. Worth digging."*

# Skyrim:Edla's House

## Overview

Edla's House

**Edla's House** is the home of [Edla](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla "Skyrim:Edla") and her son [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

It is on the north side of the village, between [Wulf Wild-Blood's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood%27s_House "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood's House") to the southwest and [Morwen's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Morwen%27s_House "Skyrim:Morwen's House") to the east.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Edla](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla "Skyrim:Edla") [Alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Alchemist")  [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)") |

### Exterior

Along the west wall is a bench, a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"), and a pen adjacent to Wulf's house holding a [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"), with a straw bale against the side of the house. Behind the house is a framed fishing net and an open shed containing a fish barrel, a rack holding five [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), and two more salmon on and next to a wooden block. Along the east wall is a partly buried crate. The entrance has a novice lock.

### Edla's House

Kitchen

The entrance leads into a room with a small fire pit with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") on a stand behind. There is a second stand with a cast iron pot containing two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot") to the right. On your left as you enter are a pair of shelves containing two [eidar cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and one of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). Hanging from the ceiling is a flat rack with three fillets of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat") and a joint of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"). On a second rack hanging from the ceiling are five salmon, a sample of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid. Under this is a narrow table with a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk") on. To the right of the entrance are two more wall shelves containing two bottles of alto wine and in a wooden bowl a piece of [honeycomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeycomb "Skyrim:Honeycomb").

Against the north wall heading to the back of the room are three small steps underneath the flight of stairs up to the top floor. On your right, under the stairs is a wood pile, a crate, two sacks and a barrel. Against the south wall is a barrel and sack, beside these is a long table and two chairs. On the table is a mead barrel, bowl of [venison stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison_Stew "Skyrim:Venison Stew"), a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a wooden plate with a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and two wooden bowls one contains a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), the other a [rabbit haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_Haunch "Skyrim:Rabbit Haunch"). In the southeast corner is a doorway to a twin bedroom. Against the back wall to the west is a wardrobe with a wooden plate containing two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and to the right of it a kettle containing a fillet of horker meat and a cabbage and a basket containing three potatoes. There is also a stool with a cast iron pot containing a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") next to a chair with a bottle of wine on the floor. Between the west wall and the stairs up is a doorway to a storage room.

On your left as you enter the storeroom is a set of shelves containing two horker tusks, a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt"). Against the north wall is a narrow table with a sack on top. Against the east wall is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") set into a table with a shelf above it containing two [potions of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength") and a sample of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"). On the left is a hanging rack with a sample of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), frost mirriam and garlic braid. To the right is a sack and barrel. Against the south wall is a set of shelves containing an eidar cheese wheel, a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), two [iron helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and a bottle of alto wine.

Entering into the twin bedroom you will find a single bed in front of you in the southeast corner and on your left another single bed against the east wall. Above this bed is a shelf containing a bowl with two [flutes](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") inside.

Loft

Upstairs looks like a typical loft. There is an open crate with three [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup") in. Behind that a fish barrel on it's side and an upright barrel with two [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") and a cup on with a small set of shelves behind them. There are crates, bucket, and baskets all over, but none holding anything interesting. There is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on one of the crates with a wood pile behind it. There are three sacks on the floor and a second small set of shelves near the back containing a copy of *[Ahzidal's Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Descent "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Descent")* and a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"). Then there is another barrel and set of shelves off to the side.

Edla

**Edla** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") alchemist living in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). She lives in [her house](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla%27s_House "Skyrim:Edla's House") with her son, [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)").

Edla is quite worried about her son, Nikulas, who wants to leave Skaal Village for a life of adventure. You can help her to convince him to stay in Skaal Village and she will be very grateful to you.

She wears a [Skaal coat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Coat "Skyrim:Skaal Coat") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Boots "Skyrim:Skaal Boots") and [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Hat "Skyrim:Skaal Hat"). She carries a [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons"), her [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Edla's House Key"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Convince Nikulas to stay in Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Convince_Nikulas_to_stay_in_Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Convince Nikulas to stay in Skaal Village")**: Counsel a [young Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)") on the dangers of life as an adventurer.
- **[Further Study](/wiki/Skyrim:Further_Study "Skyrim:Further Study")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Collect a fish to help an alchemist experiment with potions. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Edla's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | [Boar Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boar_Meat "Skyrim:Boar Meat") |  |
| 1 | [Horker Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat") |  |
| ~3 | [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") | Max 4 (4@75%) |
| ~4 | [Dragonborn Ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| 5 | Common Inn [Food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |  |
| 5 | [Raw Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Raw_Meat "Skyrim:Food") |  |
| ~8 | Common [Ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") | Max 10 (10@75%) |

## Dialogue

After freeing the Wind Stone from Miraak's control, she may say:

:   *"Who are you? What am I doing here?"*
:   *"This... this is some dark magic. It has to be."*

Back in Skaal Village, her greetings are as follows:

:   *"I have goods to offer, if you have need."*
:   *"It's been many winters since my husband returned to the All-Maker, but my heart still aches from the loss."*
:   *"It brings me great comfort to know that Nikulas will stay. I thank you, outsider."*
:   *"My son and I gather items to trade with travelers who visit the village."*
:   *"My son's heart was restless. He wanted to see the world beyond our lands, and nothing I said could change his mind."*
:   *"My son's heart is restless. He wants to see the world beyond our lands, and nothing I say will change his mind."*

:   **Who do you trade with?**
:   *"Many hunters pass through our village, and sometimes the [Dark Elves](/wiki/Lore:Dunmer "Lore:Dunmer") of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") visit us. They bring us things from their homeland that we can't find on the island, such as spices, fine cloth and ores that we cannot mine here. It's true we Skaal prefer a simpler life than some, but we do still enjoy a luxury from time to time."*

:   **What have you got for sale?**

    :   *"Mostly things from the village or the land around it. Have a look."*
    :   *"Among other things, I have some fresh bread I baked this morning and vegetables from Finna's garden."*
    :   *"I gathered some plants that are useful for making potions, but I have other goods as well."*

Her goodbyes:

:   *"I am grateful for your interest in my goods."*
:   *"Be always warm, Skaal-friend."*
:   *"May the sun light your path."*
:   *"All-Maker bless you, friend of the Skaal."*
:   *"Thank you, outsider."*

### Convince Nikulas to stay in Skaal Village

:   **Who's your son?**
:   *"His name is Nikulas. He's a good lad, strong and loyal. I only wish he wasn't so eager to leave the village. I've tried to tell him that the world beyond our lands is dangerous and cruel, but he won't listen."*

:   :   **I could talk to him.**
    :   *"You would do that? I know he would listen to you. You've been out there in the wide world. You know its perils. Yes, perhaps you can convince him. I would be grateful if you would do this thing, outsider."*

:   :   **Maybe you should let him go.**
    :   *"Perhaps someday I will have to, but for now I need Nikulas here. You see, his father, my husband, was recently lost to us. Nikulas is all that I have left in this world. I know it is selfish of me to say so, but I cannot lose him. Not while I still grieve. Also, I know his heart. Nikulas is reckless and foolish, like most young men. He cannot understand what awaits him in the wide world."*

After offering to help, if you speak to her, she will have a couple new greetings:

:   *"If Nikulas leaves me now, I will be truly alone."*
:   *"If Nikulas leaves, I fear he will never return."*
:   *"I hope that you can make my son see wisdom."*

Once you return:

:   **Nikulas has agreed to stay.**
:   *"May the All-Maker bless you with many sons and daughters, outsider. Once again you have shown that you are a true friend of the Skaal. I wish that I could give you a reward that is equal to the joy in my heart, but I don't have much to offer one who has so much already. Perhaps these will prove useful to you. These herbs are unique to the island, and their like cannot be found elsewhere."*

### The Gardener of Men

Edla will witness [Storn](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider")'s death at the hands of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora"), where she will exclaim:

:   *"All-Maker save us!"*

She will approach the body to pay her respects.

:   **Edla:** *"We won't forget what you did for us, Storn Crag-Strider. Walk with the All-Maker."*

If you speak to her, she'll say:

:   *"You will stop... whatever that was - so that that evil does not swallow the Skaal like it did Storn?"*

:   *"What next? When will it stop?"*

Ehlhiel

**Ehlhiel** is a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") who may be encountered during the quest [Double-Edged](/wiki/Skyrim:Double-Edged "Skyrim:Double-Edged") if you decide to help [Zaharia](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaharia "Skyrim:Zaharia") kill him.

Ehlhiel wears a set of [monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Monk Robes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Boots"). He has a leveled one-handed weapon and a [Potion of Plentiful Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"). He knows some leveled spells: one or two frost spells, one or two healing spells, a [ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward_(spells) "Skyrim:Ward (spells)") spell, an [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_(spells) "Skyrim:Armor (spells)") spell, and one or two [reanimation](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate_(spells) "Skyrim:Reanimate (spells)") spells, and may know a [turn undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Turn_Undead_(spells) "Skyrim:Turn Undead (spells)") spell.

## Related Quests

- **[Double-Edged](/wiki/Skyrim:Double-Edged "Skyrim:Double-Edged")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Leather "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Leather"): Determine the fate of a Thalmor agent.

Eigorn

Eigorn is a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") who can be found at [Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout") as part of the [Divine Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club").

He wears the [Fastened Shield of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastened_Shield_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Fastened Shield of the Crusader"), [Reforged Boots of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Reforged_Boots_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Reforged Boots of the Crusader"), [Reforged Cuirass of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Reforged_Cuirass_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Reforged Cuirass of the Crusader"), [Reforged Gauntlets of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Reforged_Gauntlets_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Reforged Gauntlets of the Crusader"), and [Reforged Helm of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Reforged_Helm_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Reforged Helm of the Crusader"). He also carries the [Sword of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Sword of the Crusader").

## Related Quests

- **[Relics of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Relics_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Relics of the Crusader")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader"): Reclaim the holy relics of Pelinal Whitestrake.

# Skyrim:Eimar

## Overview

| Eimar (RefID: 000B2978) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | | |
| House | [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000B2978 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000B2977 |
| Other Information | | | |

| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 60 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed"), [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |

| Voice Type | [MaleYoungEager](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleYoungEager "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleYoungEager") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CWPrepareCityCitizenCityCenterExlusion](/wiki/Skyrim:CWPrepareCityCitizenCityCenterExlusion "Skyrim:CWPrepareCityCitizenCityCenterExlusion"); [CrimeFactionWhiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionWhiterun "Skyrim:CrimeFactionWhiterun"); [HonningbrewMeaderyFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:HonningbrewMeaderyFaction "Skyrim:HonningbrewMeaderyFaction") | | |

Eimar working in the Honningbrew Meadery

**Eimar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") who works at the [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery").

He wakes at 6am for a one-hour breakfast, then starts his workday. During work, he can usually be found sitting at the bar, drinking, or cleaning the place. He takes a break at noon to eat for one hour. His workday ends at 8pm, when he has a four-hour dinner before going to bed at midnight.

Eimar wears farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006C1D8 "Skyrim:Clothes") with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0003452F "Skyrim:Boots"). He wields a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") in combat.

## Related Quests

- **[Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits")**: Put [Maven Black-Briar's](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") competition out of business.

## Dialogue

Eimar seems very happy with his job and has nothing but praise when speaking to him:

:   *"If you need to sample some of the finest mead in Skyrim, you're in the right place."*
:   *"If you're looking to purchase any mead, speak to the owner, [Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn "Skyrim:Sabjorn")."*
:   *"We're a small meadery, but growing quickly. Sabjorn's only been running this place for a short time now and look at it."*
:   *"[Mallus](/wiki/Skyrim:Mallus_Maccius "Skyrim:Mallus Maccius") is teaching me everything he knows about brewing. Hopefully, I can take over his position some day."*

However, after the quest [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits"), he will no longer be as enthusiastic:

:   *"It's a shame the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery") took this place over. I never liked it as much as our [Honningbrew](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead")."*
:   *"If you're looking to purchase any mead, speak to the brewmaster, Mallus."*

## Bugs

- During Dampened Spirits, Eimar has some lines at the [Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") that don't make sense for him to use while he's there. One wasn't conditioned to the location he's in, and the other was using an incorrect function to check if the latter is finished or not.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, fixes this bug.

Einarth

**Einarth**, an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest"), is one of the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") living at [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"). He will teach you the second [word](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_of_Power "Skyrim:Word of Power") of the Unrelenting Force shout. At the end of the quest [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall"), Einarth can be heard lecturing [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") when the latter refuses to help you in your quest to learn the [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") shout, saying: *"Arngeir. Rok los Dovahkiin, Strundu'ul. Rok fen tinvaak Paarthurnax."*

Einarth wears a set of [Greybeard's robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeard%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Greybeard's Robes") with the matching [hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeard%27s_Hood "Skyrim:Greybeard's Hood") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeard%27s_Boots "Skyrim:Greybeard's Boots"). He carries a copy of the book *[Dwemer History and Culture](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_History_and_Culture "Skyrim:Dwemer History and Culture")*, a bottle of [Black-Briar Reserve](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Reserve "Skyrim:Black-Briar Reserve"), a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), one sample of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), and three [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips").

He knows the following shouts: [Disarm](/wiki/Skyrim:Disarm "Skyrim:Disarm"), [Dismay](/wiki/Skyrim:Dismay "Skyrim:Dismay"), [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury"), [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath"), [Frost Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Breath "Skyrim:Frost Breath"), [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form"), [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"), and [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint").

## Related Quests

- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").
- **[The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller")**: Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").
- **[The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World")**: Receive a lesson from [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
- **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").
- **[Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)")**: Deal with a [potential threat](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").

## Notes

- Of the Greybeards, Einarth has the lowest level of 90. [Wulfgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulfgar "Skyrim:Wulfgar") and [Borri](/wiki/Skyrim:Borri "Skyrim:Borri") are at level 100, while Arngeir is level 150.

Eirid

**Eirid** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") living in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Her parents are [Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") and [Dagur](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagur "Skyrim:Dagur"), and they run [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") inn. She wanders the inn from 8am to noon, goes outside to play till 6pm then returns to the inn and sleeps in the basement at night.

Eirid wears red colored [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") and a small amount of gold.

## Dialogue

:   *"There's not many people left in Winterhold, so I only have Assur to play with, and sometimes he's mean."*
:   *"He always wants to play 'Hunt the Elf', and he makes me be the elf."*
:   *"Assur says his pa says the College made lots of bad things happen, but the mages I've seen look nice."*
:   *"The mages don't let us go in the College. They said it's not safe in there."*
:   *"Assur and I are playing a game. Don't tell him where I am!"*

Should the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") take over Winterhold, Assur and [his](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") [family](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaena "Skyrim:Thaena") will be exiled. Eirid can be found commenting on this:

:   *"Assur had to move away because of the Empire. But we get to stay."*

Should you talk to Eirid during [Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment"), where Winterhold is disrupted by [Magic Anomalies](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly"), she will be scared:

:   *"Did you make something bad happen?"*

## Conversations

Her parents can be heard discussing putting an end to Assur and Eirid playing 'Hunt the Elf':

:   **Haran**: *"I understand Eirid's been playing 'Hunt the Elf' again."*
:   **Dagur**: *"It's just children playing, Haran. I wouldn't fret over it."*
:   **Haran**: *"I'm not 'fretting.' I don't want Eirid playing those sorts of games!"*
:   **Dagur**: *"All right, all right. I'll speak to her."*

## Notes

- The "Hunt the Elf" scene between Eirid and Assur does not work due to invalid condition checks.

## Bugs

- Eirid's bed is scaled down too far, causing her to float above it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Although Eirid is scheduled to go play outside, this does not occur. She simply goes to bed at noon and sleeps till 8am. **?**

| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 95-258 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")**, **[Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed")**, [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Aggressive |
| [Protected](/wiki/Skyrim:Protected_NPCs "Skyrim:Protected NPCs") | Yes | | |
| Voice Type | [FemaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [dunFrostmereCryptEisaFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DunFrostmereCryptEisaFaction "Skyrim:DunFrostmereCryptEisaFaction") | | |

Eisa outside Frostmere Crypt

Eisa in the Moorside Inn after making it safely to Morthal

**Eisa Blackthorn** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") living in Skyrim. After a year in [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine") she became a member of the White River Gang, a group of bandits in [White River Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Watch "Skyrim:White River Watch") led by [Hajvarr Iron-Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Hajvarr_Iron-Hand "Skyrim:Hajvarr Iron-Hand"). She and the others were forced to flee after a failed mutiny. Eisa went to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") along with [Ra'jirr](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27jirr "Skyrim:Ra'jirr") where they heard about a group of treasure hunters near [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). After joining [Kyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyr "Skyrim:Kyr")'s band in [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt") she was put in charge of the dig and soon after discovered an underground forest. In the forest they discovered a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Blade "Skyrim:The Pale Blade") on some kind of monument, which Kyr kept for himself. After the sword had been removed Ra'jirr began hallucinating about the [Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady_(creature) "Skyrim:The Pale Lady (creature)") and decided to steal the sword and return it to the forest. Kyr assumed Eisa and Ra'jirr had stolen the sword together and put out a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyr%27s_Bounty "Skyrim:Kyr's Bounty") of 100 gold for both of them.

Eisa will be found being attacked by her fellow bandits outside Frostmere Crypt. You may assist her, but you will be able to acquire her related quest regardless of your actions. If she survives the encounter at the crypt, she will follow the road and end up at the [Moorside Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Moorside_Inn "Skyrim:Moorside Inn") in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). Healing her along the way will be taken as an act of aggression and cause her to attack.

Eisa wears a full set of [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), including a pair of steel gauntlets (two variants), and a pair of steel boots (two variants). She is equipped with a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality) and a leveled [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") (up to [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel") quality). She carries a leveled [potion of restore health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a 25% chance of a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), and a small amount of gold.

## Related Quests

- **[The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady")**: Find out what happened in [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt").

## Quest-Related Dialogue

As you approach Frostmere Crypt you will see her being attacked by her fellow bandits:

:   **Eisa:** *"Damn it, not now!"*
:   **Bandit:** *"There she is!"*
:   **Bandit:** *"Get her!"*

If she survives she will approach you:

:   *"Who in Dagon's name are you? Speak, or I'll cut you down where you stand."*

:   :   **Wait, what's going on here?**
    :   *"\*Sigh\* I was part of the gang in the ruins here. Friend of mine went crazy and stole the boss' sword. They blamed me for it. Look, I'm done here. Mop the floor with these idiots for all I care. Just get out of my way."*

:   :   **Let's just see about that.**
    :   *"Hmph. Suit yourself."*

## Notes

- Two prisoners in Cidhna Mine, [Braig](/wiki/Skyrim:Braig "Skyrim:Braig") and [Grisvar the Unlucky](/wiki/Skyrim:Grisvar_the_Unlucky "Skyrim:Grisvar the Unlucky") still mention Eisa, seemingly misremembering her last name:

:   **Grisvar**: *"Hey, remember that girl, Eisa? The one who sliced open that pickpocket they threw in here?"*
:   **Braig**: *"The Blackblood*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *girl? Now there was a fighter. If I didn't know better, I'd say she was a Forsworn woman."*

## Bugs

- It's possible to find Eisa standing outside Frostmere Crypt, unharmed and alone. In order to get her journal and trigger her quest, you have to either pickpocket or kill her. If you attempt to enter and exit the crypt with her standing outside, she may disappear from the game.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
  - Reload an earlier save file where you are far from the location and approach Frostmere Crypt from the west road to trigger the event in which three bandits should be attacking Eisa. An option is to fast travel to Morthal and then approach her location from the road coming from there.
- Bandits may not attack her and the quest will not start.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
  - To fix this, pickpocket and read her journal.
  - You can also fix this by jumping down from the path above Frostmere Crypt.
- She may become permanently aggressive toward you upon entry to the Moorside Inn. Since she attacks first, you can slay her in self defense (and not get a bounty), then loot her journal and read it to trigger the quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.9, addresses this issue. Her aggression level there was set too high.
- If you kill her outside of Frostmere Crypt, then bring her inside as a dead thrall, she might blink out of existence shortly after entering.

Elberon's Apprentice

**Elberon's Apprentice** is a hostile mage who will appear in the Vardnknd Gallery section of [Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") during the related quest, alongside several hostile mercenaries. He is the apprentice of [Elberon](/wiki/Skyrim:Elberon "Skyrim:Elberon"), a [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") wizard who is fatally struck by lightning when you first enter Vardnknd Gallery.

He is wearing [Apprentice Robes of Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Apprentice_Robes_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Apprentice Robes of Illusion"), an [apprentice hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Apprentice_Hood "Skyrim:Apprentice Hood"), and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), and wields a [Dwarven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"). He can use the [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt"), [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward") and [Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(spell) "Skyrim:Invisibility (spell)") spells.

He uses generic [bandit dialogue](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit#Dialogue "Skyrim:Bandit").

## Related Quests

- **[Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"): Shut down a malfunctioning Dwarven weather machine.

# Skyrim:Elberon

## Overview

| Level | 2 | Class | [Dremora Class](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes#Dremora "Skyrim:Classes") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | [xx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")001715 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | [xx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")0008EE |

| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |

Elberon

Elberon Blackthorn is a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") wizard who has entered the ruins of [Vardnknd](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") to shut down the malfunctioning Weather Witch within before it can threaten all of Skyrim. He has hired a band of hostile mercenaries to clear the ruins, and has set up camp in Vardnknd Gallery. However, this section of the ruins is currently being subjected to constant lightning strikes, and upon entering Vardnknd Gallery you will witness Elberon being struck by a lightning bolt while sitting at his desk, killing him instantly. His death will trigger the quest [The Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:The Dwarven Crown").

He is wearing [Adept Robes of Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Adept_Robes_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Adept Robes of Illusion"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), and a strange [Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown"), the latter of which you will be required to loot as part of the quest The Dwarven Crown. He also carries his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Elberon%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Elberon's Journal"), which you will need to read as part of the quest [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)").

After you have recovered all four [Vardnknd Conduit Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Vardnknd_Conduit_Gem "Skyrim:Vardnknd Conduit Gem"), [Elberon's Apprentice](/wiki/Skyrim:Elberon%27s_Apprentice "Skyrim:Elberon's Apprentice") will appear in Vardnknd Gallery along with several more mercenaries and will attack you on sight.

## Related Quests

- **[The Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:The Dwarven Crown")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"): Gather all the components of a powerful Dwarven Crown from within a [forgotten Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns").
- **[Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"): Shut down a malfunctioning Dwarven weather machine.

## Notes

- He is the author of *[Elberon's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Elberon%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Elberon's Journal")* and *[Forgotten Seasons, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons,_v1 "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons, v1")*.

Elda Early-Dawn

**Elda Early-Dawn** is the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") proprietor of [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). She will rent out a room to you for 10 gold a night and offers merchant services. If anything happens to Elda, [Nils](/wiki/Skyrim:Nils "Skyrim:Nils") takes over running Candlehearth Hall.

She spends her entire life behind the counter, selling food and drink to the regulars. She only makes an exception if you rent a bed for the night and will then escort you to your room. She wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#_0001be1b "Skyrim:Clothing"). She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

When you approach her, she will welcome you to Candlehearth Hall:

:   *"This here's Candlehearth Hall. Great room's upstairs, an' there's a bed for rent on the ground floor."*

However, if you are a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") she will instead mock you:

:   *"Another Dark Elf. Just what Windhelm needs."*

:   *"Maybe you should just move along."*

Her other greetings are more polite, for all races:

:   *"Got some fresh-baked bread an' good cheese, if you're after a bite to eat"*

:   *"Mind you don't get fresh with [Susanna](/wiki/Skyrim:Susanna_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Susanna the Wicked"). She plays the flirt, but it's just to get good tips."*

For non-Dunmer, she may also add:

:   *"Those Dark Elf refugees will take over the city if we aren't careful."*

You can ask her about the name of the inn to which she'll respond in a condescending tone:

:   **Why is this called Candlehearth Hall?**
:   *"Did you see that candle above the fire upstairs? It was lit one hundred and sixty-three years ago, back when this building was the home of a grand warrior named Vundheim. When word came that he'd fallen, his son Deroct lit the candle in his honor. Nobody knows why it still burns."*

Once she has escorted you to your room, she will say one of the following:

:   *"Enjoy your stay, and don't break nothin'!"*

:   *"Mind you don't put out that candle on the hearth upstairs!"*

When asked for rumors, she may tell you about the [Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") boy in town:

:   **Heard any rumors lately?**
:   *"Folk been hearing some strange stuff coming from the Aretino place. Chanting. Talk is, little Aventus is trying to contact the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood")..."*

When asked about magic she will point you to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"):

:   **Where can I learn more about magic?**
:   *"Magic? Goodness, not here! Nothing dangerous like that! That's all kept to that College up in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Better that than dealing with [Ulfric's wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") like some do."*

If the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") ends with the death of [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), you can ask her if she misses him, which she will confirm:

:   **Do you miss Ulfric Stormcloak?**
:   *"Aye, that I do. I ain't sayin' he was perfect, but he knew what it meant to be a Nord. [The Empire's](/wiki/Lore:Empire "Lore:Empire") always taken us for granted. Nords died by the thousands in the [Great War](/wiki/Lore:Wars#Great_War "Lore:Wars"), and what did the Empire do? They outlawed the worship of [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos"), Skyrim's most beloved son. There's thanks for you. I guess what I'm sayin' is, Ulfric stood up for us, an' for all Skyrim. So who's goin' to stand up for us now?"*

## Conversations

Elda will randomly have brief conversations with the regulars at Candlehearth Hall, specifically [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium"), [Captain Lonely-Gale](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Lonely-Gale "Skyrim:Captain Lonely-Gale"), and [Jora](/wiki/Skyrim:Jora "Skyrim:Jora"):

*"Calixto, do you know if there's any truth to these rumors of dragons?"*

*"Captain, have you heard these stories of dragons?"*

:   **Elda**: *"Calixto, do you know if there's any truth to these rumors of dragons?"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Eh. I try not to trouble myself with stories of the outside world. Now if someone brings me a dragon scale, that's a different story."*
:   **Elda**: *"But how would you know it's real?"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Ah, I can't reveal all my secrets to you. But rest assured, I would know."*

:   **Elda**: *"Calixto, someone left an interesting ring in here a few weeks ago. Would you like a look?"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Of course, my dear. It may prove to be quite the curiosity! One must always be alert."*
:   **Elda**: *"Well, I seem to have misplaced it at the moment. But it was white, like alabaster, with three bright rubies set in it."*
:   **Calixto**: *"Be very careful with that. It sounds as if it may be the Death Ring of Dro'farahn. A ring of the most dangerous sort."*
:   **Elda**: *"Oh dear. What should I do?"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Bring it to me straight away when you find it. Don't dally. I can keep it safe."*
:   **Elda**: *"Oh, thank the gods you're in Windhelm, Calixto!"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Think nothing of it."*

:   **Elda**: *"Captain, have you heard these stories of dragons?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Elda, you know better than to believe every idiot traveler that wanders through."*
:   **Elda**: *"But they're saying that one of them freed Ulfric... that he's in league with them."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Think about how ridiculous that sounds. Come now."*

:   **Elda**: *"So what's the news on the street, Captain?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"The dark elves are uneasy. There's a killer on the streets. And Viola Giordano won't leave me alone."*
:   **Elda**: *"How would you like a drink?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Very much so."*
:   **Elda**: *"Coming right up."*

:   **Elda**: *"Oh, Jora. Good to see you. I was wondering if you might ask Lortheim something for me."*
:   **Jora**: *"Don't bother. I don't have much chance of seeing my husband these days. He's always up in the palace with Ulfric."*
:   **Elda**: *"Oh, I'm sorry to hear that. Is everything all right?"*
:   **Jora**: *"It's been better, I'll be honest with you."*
:   **Elda**: *"Here, let me get you some mead. This one's on me."*

:   **Jora**: *"I just don't know what to do anymore. He's hardly ever in the temple. I see him at breakfast, and that's it."*
:   **Elda**: *"I know, dear. He's a busy man, though, and loyal to the Stormcloaks."*
:   **Jora**: *"What about being loyal to his wife?"*
:   **Elda**: *"I... I'm sorry, dear, I've got some other customers. I'll be back around in a minute."*

She also has a relationship with [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter"), who talks about settling down with her:

:   **Brunwulf**: *"I've been thinking about building that cabin we talked about."*
:   **Elda**: *"Oh? Where?"*
:   **Brunwulf**: *"There's a clear spot just west of Riften. You know the area?"*
:   **Elda**: *"I've been there before, but I don't know it well."*
:   **Brunwulf**: *"Well that's where I want to build. In the fall forest. Give it an easterly view. The sunrise is almost as pretty as you are."*
:   **Elda**: *"That sounds lovely. You're very sweet."*

:   **Brunwulf**: *"How long have you run this place, again?"*
:   **Elda**: *"Nearly thirty years, now."*
:   **Brunwulf**: *"Just wondering when you'll be ready to give it up and settle down. Seems like you're always working."*
:   **Elda**: *"I just feel like if I'm not here, then something could go wrong. Nils is a hard worker, but I wouldn't trust him to run things."*
:   **Brunwulf**: *"One of these days he'll have to learn."*

:   **Elda**: *"Tell me about the Great War. I hear you were in the battle of..."*
:   **Brunwulf**: *"Elda, honey, let's not talk about the war. It's in the past."*
:   **Elda**: *"I'm sorry. What would you like to talk about?"*
:   **Brunwulf**: *"Hows*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *about we figure out some way to keep warm tonight?"*
:   **Elda**: *"Oh! You behave, now!"*

## Notes

- Elda was supposed to a play a part in the [unfinished quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests") [Supply Line](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests#Supply_Line "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"). However, since the quest can never be started, Elda's dialogue, *"Ah, good. I've been waiting on that. Here's the gold for it. Thanks."* will never be heard.

## Bugs

- Elda will still remind you to keep your hands off of Susanna even after you have finished [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Elda's vendor chest doesn't always stock bread despite her saying she sells it consistently.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Elder Knowledge

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)") |
| Location(s): | [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"),  [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple") or [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"),  [Septimus Signus's Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus%27s_Outpost "Skyrim:Septimus Signus's Outpost"),  [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"), [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"),  [Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark"). |
| Reward: | [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") |
| ID: | MQ205 |
| Suggested Level: | 18 |
| Difficulty: | Hard |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") | **Concurrent** [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane") | **Next →** [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") | | Concurrent | [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane") | | → Next | [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane") | | |

Hidden, deep within [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"), lies an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Scrolls "Lore:Elder Scrolls")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Accept the task from [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
2. (Optional) Talk to [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") or [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir").
3. Read through the rare books provided by [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").
4. Receive the necessary items from [Septimus Signus](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Septimus Signus").
5. Locate the ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") city of [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach").
6. Claim the [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Scroll "Lore:Elder Scroll").

### Fragments of Creation

[Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Lore:Alduin%27s_Wall "Lore:Alduin's Wall") documents how the ancient [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") of the [First Era](/wiki/Lore:First_Era "Lore:First Era") used a special [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") to help them dispose of [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin"). Your search for this particular shout takes you to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar") and eventually to the leader of the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards"), the dragon [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)"). He reveals that the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Lore:Throat_of_the_World "Lore:Throat of the World") was indeed the battleground where the ancient Nords fought Alduin and ended the [Dragon War](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_War "Lore:Dragon War"). He also reveals that the [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") shout was not enough to truly defeat Alduin, in reality merely crippling him. In a final attempt to banish Alduin, the Nords were forced to use an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Scroll "Lore:Elder Scroll") to send their foe forward in time, postponing the threat, but not ending it. The event created a rift in time itself atop the mountain, known as the Time-Wound. Paarthurnax believes that, in order to learn the Dragonrend shout, you will have to locate the Elder Scroll, then use it to open the Time-Wound and learn the shout from the ancient Nords that created it. To begin your lengthy quest for the legendary Scroll, you will need to talk to either [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") or [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *"If the world is meant to end, so be it."*  **Arngeir's Warning** If you choose to question Arngeir about obtaining an Elder Scroll, you will find him inside High Hrothgar, where he will be reading, meditating, or sleeping. Arngeir is more skeptical than Esbern about the necessity of learning the Dragonrend shout and, when asked how one would find an Elder Scroll, he will vehemently protest: *"Such blasphemies are the calling of mages, not followers of the Way. Take your question to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"). They may be able to help you."* When asked if there is another way to defeat Alduin, he will explain his uncertainty: *"Perhaps not. But this Shout was used once before, was it not? And here we are again. Have you considered that Alduin was not meant to be defeated? Those who overthrew him in ancient times only postponed the day of reckoning, they did not stop it. If the world is meant to end, so be it. Let it end and be reborn."* | *"The whole world was in darkness."*  **Esbern's Dream** If you choose to visit Esbern, you will find him outside [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"), where he and [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") can be seen staring into the horizon as Esbern recalls a strange dream he once had about Alduin. After the story, Esbern will greet you as if he only just realized your presence: *"Ah, you're back. I hope you've made some progress on tracking down this Shout we need to defeat Alduin?"* You can then explain that you need an Elder Scroll in order to learn Dragonrend. He will be intrigued: *"Ah, indeed? There's a pretty puzzle. Not the kind of thing you'll find in your local bookshop. Let me think... Perhaps the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). What learning there is in Skyrim is gathered there. One of the mages there may be able to put you on the trail of this Elder Scroll."* |

### An Incomprehensible Book

Urag gro-Shub and his two books on the Elder Scrolls

Make your way to the College of Winterhold. If you have not joined the College, you will be forced to start the initiation quest, [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons"), to get past gatekeeper [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda"). If you are already a member, enter the College as normal and follow your map marker to the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"). Here you will find the librarian [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"). After belittling you for your ignorance, he will fill you in on the potential dangers of the Scrolls: *"An Elder Scroll is an instrument of immense knowledge and power. To read an Elder Scroll, a person must have the most rigorously trained mind, or else risk madness. Even so, the Divines usually take the reader's sight as a price."* He will then elaborate on the incredible nature of the Elder Scrolls: *"The simplest way to put it is "knowledge," but there's nothing simple about an Elder Scroll. It's a reflection of all possible futures and all possible pasts. Each reader sees different reflections through different lenses, and may come away with a very different reading. But at the same time, all of it is true. Even the falsehoods. Especially the falsehoods."* You can also ask him who wrote the Elder Scrolls and he will respond: *"It would take a month to explain to you how that very question doesn't even make sense. The Scrolls exist here, with us, but also beyond and beneath. Before and after. They are bits of Divine made substance so we could know them. Some people who study them devoutly go mad."*

Naturally, Urag does not have a Scroll lying around, and he wouldn't simply give it to you if he had. After a short discussion, Urag leaves his spot behind the counter and fetches two rare books for you, *[Ruminations on the Elder Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruminations_on_the_Elder_Scrolls "Skyrim:Ruminations on the Elder Scrolls")* and *[Effects of the Elder Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Effects_of_the_Elder_Scrolls "Skyrim:Effects of the Elder Scrolls")*. The first book is written by [Septimus Signus](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Septimus Signus") and starts the concurrent quest [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane") when opened. When you tell Urag that Signus's book is incomprehensible, he will explain that Septimus Signus is a specialist in Elder Scrolls lore, but he has not been back to the College for a long time. He mentions that Signus became obsessed with the [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") and took off north to study an old artifact.

### Beyond the Physical World

Septimus Signus and the Dwemer lockbox

From this point, the quest Discerning the Transmundane will be part of your quest to claim the Elder Scroll. Follow your map marker to a remote ice cavern named [Septimus Signus's Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus%27s_Outpost "Skyrim:Septimus Signus's Outpost") and enter. Inside you will find Septimus Signus pacing before a huge device with a strange-looking lock, muttering to himself about the Dwemer. When questioned on the Elder Scrolls, his answer will be just as incomprehensible as his book: *"Elder Scrolls. Indeed. The Empire. They absconded with them. Or so they think. The ones they saw. The ones they thought they saw. I know of one. Forgotten. Sequestered. But I cannot go to it, not poor Septimus, for I... I have arisen beyond its grasp."* When you inquire as to the location of the Scroll, he will respond: *"Here. Well, here as in this plane. Mundus. Tamriel. Nearby, relatively speaking. On the cosmological scale, it's all nearby."* He will then agree to help you, but only if you help him, naturally. He'll point towards the Dwemer lockbox in the icy cavern and say: *"You see this masterwork of the Dwemer. Deep inside their greatest knowings. Septimus is clever among men, but he is but an idiot child compared to the dullest of the Dwemer. Lucky then they left behind their own way of reading the Elder Scrolls. In the depths of [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") one yet lies."* He will explain what Blackreach is and what you must go through: *"Under deep. Below the dark. The hidden keep. [Tower Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark"). [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"). The point of puncture, of first entry, of the tapping. Delve to its limits, and Blackreach lies just beyond. But not all can enter there. Only Septimus knows the hidden key to loose the lock to jump beneath the deathly rock."*

While it is clear that Septimus doesn't care about the Elder Scroll itself, it is quite clear that he needs the information it possesses. You will have no choice but to help him. He will hand you two items, the [Blank Lexicon](/wiki/Skyrim:Blank_Lexicon "Skyrim:Blank Lexicon") and the [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere"). A knowledgeable person indeed, he will then provide his complex explanation on what to do with the items, including a tip that will prove valuable [later](#The_Elder_Scroll). He will also provide his knowledge on what defines an Elder Scroll: *"You look to your left, you see one way. You look to your right, you see another. But neither is any harder than the opposite. But the Elder Scrolls... they look left and right in the stream of time. The future and past are as one. Sometimes they even look up. What do they see then? What if they dive in? Then the madness begins."*

**NOTE**: While the map marker will point you towards Alftand, you can gain access to Blackreach from two other [ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins"), specifically [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft") and [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar"). However, if you have yet to clear either of those, the route through Alftand is recommended as your map marker will point you in the right direction.

### Alftand

[Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand")

The Dwemer ruin of [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand") is located southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). The exterior area contains a deserted camp, but upon investigating the ruined shack near the campsite, you will find an *[Expedition Manifest](/wiki/Skyrim:Expedition_Manifest "Skyrim:Expedition Manifest")* written by expedition leader [Sulla Trebatius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sulla_Trebatius "Skyrim:Sulla Trebatius"), hinting that you may not be alone when traversing Alftand. From the shack, head down the slope and enter the first zone, [Alftand Glacial Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand_Glacial_Ruins "Skyrim:Alftand Glacial Ruins").

#### The Lost Expedition

The icy tunnel ahead contains no enemies but plenty of destroyed cooking spits, and before long you will see blood spatters all over the floor. A little further down the tunnel, you will hear the voice of one of the [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") members of the expedition in a [Skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma")-induced rant, demanding that his companion tell him where the rest of the Skooma is hidden. Head east through the tunnel and follow the path as it twists and turns. You will soon arrive in a room with a table and [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo")'s book *[Dwarves, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarves,_v2 "Skyrim:Dwarves, v2")* along with some *[Research Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Research_Notes "Skyrim:Research Notes")* from Sulla Trebatius. The door to the north is barred, so take the western path and fight the dwarven automatons that guard it. As the tunnel becomes icy again, you will encounter [J'darr](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27darr "Skyrim:J'darr"), mad from Skooma withdrawal, who will attack you on sight. In the corner, you will find the corpse of his brother [J'zhar](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zhar "Skyrim:J'zhar"), lying in a pool of his own blood.

Leave the bodies behind and head north until you reach a chamber with two [dwarven spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere"). Proceed forward. To the left, there are a set of rising and falling platforms. If you manage to get onto the tallest of the three, there will be two unlocked chests, with several potions and a jewel on a nearby surface. Then proceed through the only available path, where you will find a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") and more [dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider"). In this room, you can find *[Umana's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Umana%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Umana's Journal")*, which describes how the dangers of Alftand have claimed even more victims. Before you open the western door, there will be a novice-locked gate containing two locked chests (adept and apprentice) and various small dwemer items. After opening the western door, beware of the [dwarven pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in front of the chest at the top of the stairs. To the right will be another [dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider"), easy to either kill or sneak past, and an adept-locked chest. From there, head south, where another spider will be waiting. Directly past it, on your left, will be a room containing a potion of minor stamina and a potion of either vigorous or extreme healing. Even further ahead on the right is an apprentice-locked door. Inside is a dwarven sphere, an unlocked chest, two beds, and various other dwarven items. Past this the hallway splits into two: on the left, a long ledge featuring [dwarven spider workers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") and pipes that could easily push you off; to the right, a solitary spider focused on attacking the wall, and a [Blacksmith's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Potion"). Climb across to the end of the ledge and proceed to the [Alftand Animonculory](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand_Animonculory "Skyrim:Alftand Animonculory").

#### The Eyeless Creatures

The Animonculory door opens up into another hallway. Turn left past the first gear in the wall to find an unlocked chest, a [Falmer helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Helmet "Skyrim:Falmer Helmet") and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Shield "Skyrim:Falmer Shield"), a hint as to your future enemies, and assorted dwemer items. Open the door at the far end and enter the enormous chamber beyond. To your right will be a distracted Dwarven Spider Worker; if you enter the small pathway next to the stairs, you will find yet another deceased expedition member, [Endrast](/wiki/Skyrim:Endrast "Skyrim:Endrast"), who is still holding his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Endrast%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Endrast's Journal"). On top of the journal are a lockpick and stick of charcoal, and opposite the body is an adept-locked chest. Retrace your steps, climb the stairs and find the slope to the east, where a Dwarven Sphere is patrolling. There are three pressure plates here that trigger a deadly set of [spinning blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades"). Dodge these and proceed to the level.

The central chamber of the [Animonculory](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand_Animonculory "Skyrim:Alftand Animonculory")

This room is the first very large, multi-leveled chamber in Alftand. You are on the top level, so start making your way down the slopes and fight the enemies as you go. The area near the beginning, as you step down the first ramp, contains a Dwarven Spider, a potion of extreme magicka, and a novice-locked chest. When you have traversed one floor, an apprentice-locked door to the east leads to some worthwhile treasure. Inside is another [Dwarven Spider Worker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider"), two other gates (One unlocked and open, with an unlocked chest imside; the other with an expert lock. Inside are two chests, one unlocked, one master-locked, two potions, a [Dwarven Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Helmet "Skyrim:Dwarven Helmet"), a skeleton, and a [book](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Locked_Room "Skyrim:The Locked Room").)You'll need to make a short jump down to proceed, where you will land near the body of [Yag gra-Gortwog](/wiki/Skyrim:Yag_gra-Gortwog "Skyrim:Yag gra-Gortwog"). To the southeast is another slope leading down, where you will find the first [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") enemy. Stay on the path and kill any Falmer that get in your way. You will reach a platform with a door and a broken pipe spitting out fire. Open the door to leave the huge chamber for now and proceed forward towards an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and several Falmer emerging from their tents. Dodge the flames coming from the pipes and head south until you reach a junction. The stairs to the east lead to a small room with some ingredients, while the path south will lead you to the next room.

In this room, the elevator on the other side of the barred doorway leads back to the previous zone, Alftand Glacial Ruins, so at this point it is possible to return to the outside world and stock up on supplies. Otherwise, skip the elevator ride and locate Sulla Trebatius's Pack. You will also find a table holding the dead body of [Valie](/wiki/Skyrim:Valie "Skyrim:Valie") and another with an array of rare ingredients, including a [small pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Pearl "Skyrim:Small Pearl"), one of only two samples in Skyrim. Find the path to the northeast and open the door. You will find yourself back in the huge central chamber, where you can continue your descent. There are three Falmer and a [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") at the bottom of the chamber; dispose of them and locate the door to the north and enter. The next area contains a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire"), which triggers a [claw trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw"). Avoid the tripwire and the trap and continue into [Alftand Cathedral](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand_Cathedral "Skyrim:Alftand Cathedral").

#### The Dwemer Mechanism

The [Cathedral](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand_Cathedral "Skyrim:Alftand Cathedral")

Alftand Cathedral is the last zone of Alftand, and the smallest as well. Upon entering, take a right turn and dodge the three [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate"), all of which will trigger a [slicer](/wiki/Skyrim:Slicer "Skyrim:Slicer") from the ceiling. Fight a single Falmer enemy and open the door to another huge chamber, where you will find more Falmer. Dispose of them, take a moment to explore the room for lots of chests and loot, then head up the stairs next to the entrance and pull the lever. This lowers the spikes blocking the gate to the west, but approach the area carefully as you will awaken a [dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion"). After the battle, loot the centurion for the [Key to Alftand Lift](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Alftand_Lift "Skyrim:Key to Alftand Lift") and head up the stairs. Open the gate where you will witness the last two survivors of the failed expedition, [Sulla Trebatius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sulla_Trebatius "Skyrim:Sulla Trebatius") and [Umana](/wiki/Skyrim:Umana "Skyrim:Umana"), having a conversation revealing Sulla's true intentions:

**Umana**: *"Sulla look, the passage is open, wait... there's someone down there!"*
**Sulla**: *"No! Blackreach was to be my discovery!"*
**Umana**: *"Sulla, let's just get out of here. Hasn't there been enough death?"*
**Sulla**: *"Oh, of course you want me to leave. Just waiting for me to turn my back. So you can have all the glory for yourself!"*

Sulla and Umana will then proceed to fight each other; keep your distance until one is victorious (usually Umana). The other will then turn against you. Dispose of them and investigate Umana's body for the unique shield [Targe of the Blooded](/wiki/Skyrim:Targe_of_the_Blooded "Skyrim:Targe of the Blooded"). Turn your attention towards the Dwarven Mechanism in the center of the room. Activate it, and the Attunement Sphere will do the rest, revealing a staircase leading downward. You can return to the outside world from here by using your newly acquired [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Alftand_Lift "Skyrim:Key to Alftand Lift") on the gate to the southwest. This will also provide a useful shortcut for later visits (make sure to open the gate at the top of the elevator). From here, head down the stairs and prepare yourself for [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach").

### Blackreach

Blackreach

The Tower of Mzark

Finally, you will be in Blackreach, a vast, beautiful, eerie, and dangerous underground cavern that will take time to traverse completely. Dwarven automatons and Falmer continue to be common enemies, and you may encounter [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") and [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") as well. Blackreach can be overwhelming and quite difficult to navigate, especially since your in-game map will only ever allow you to see a portion of the cavern. Additionally, it is loaded with distractions, so stay on the path for now and keep your eye on the prize: the Elder Scroll.

The fastest route from Alftand to the Tower of Mzark is the road to the left, immediately out of the Alftand Cathedral. Continue along the road in a southeastern direction and fight a dwarven sphere and a Falmer. When you come to the first junction, make a right and head southwest along that road and fight more chaurus and another Falmer. As you travel underneath a bridge, a Falmer will shoot arrows at you from above, but just move forward and stay on the path. Fight two chaurus and continue on until the path turns in a western direction, across a bridge. When you cross the bridge, the Tower of Mzark will be visible to the southwest, and the trail will lead you right to the entrance.

### The Elder Scroll

The Elder Scroll recovered

Once you have entered the Tower of Mzark, investigate the first room for some minor loot. The [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Armorer's Challenge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Armorer%27s_Challenge "Skyrim:The Armorer's Challenge")* is located in the west facing corner of the room (to the right of the doorway on the far wall). Proceed through the door and behold a Dwemer contraption that would make even Septimus Signus proud: a giant sphere with various lenses fills the entire first floor of the room. The second floor sits on the upper part of the sphere and, hanging from the ceiling, a series of lenses conceal a container. If you investigate the surrounding area, you will find the skeletal remains of [Drokt](/wiki/Skyrim:Drokt "Skyrim:Drokt"). His [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Journal_of_Drokt "Skyrim:Journal of Drokt") will inform you how he became obsessed with the Oculory, and he seemingly died without managing to align it correctly. The journal also contains a tip on how to solve the puzzle: *"The light through the knowledge through the machine rests on the cube."* This echoes the words of Septimus Signus: *"The Dwemer found a loophole, as they always do. To focus the knowledge away and inside without harm. Place the lexicon into their contraption and focus the knowings into it."*

With these two tips in mind, head up the last slope, where you will find four buttons and a Lexicon Receptacle. Place the Blank Lexicon in the receptacle and watch the ceiling of the room open, shining light onto the container beneath. This also activates the two buttons on the right. To focus the lenses on the floor, place yourself so you can see the Lexicon and the central floor. Activate the button on the second pedestal from the right four times in a row and the Lexicon will open. This also activates one of the buttons to the left. Press the second button from the left twice and the lenses in the ceiling will change position, allowing the light shining through the container to hit the corresponding lenses on the floor, thus filling the Lexicon with knowledge. The last button to the left will now be active, so push it once and the upper lenses will move aside, making room for the container to be lowered down from the ceiling. Once it has reached the floor, it will open and reveal the legendary Elder Scroll (Dragon), the very source of the elder knowledge, yours for the taking. Remember to pick up the inscribed [Runed Lexicon](/wiki/Skyrim:Runed_Lexicon "Skyrim:Runed Lexicon") from the receptacle, then claim the Elder Scroll. This ends the quest and starts the next one, [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane").

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **Elder Knowledge** (20 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- Attempting to read the Elder Scroll will inflict temporary blindness upon you.
- Having the [Clairvoyance](/wiki/Skyrim:Clairvoyance_(spell) "Skyrim:Clairvoyance (spell)") spell can be very helpful for navigating Blackreach.
- If you have already spoken to Urag gro-Shub, you will have an option to tell Paarthurnax that the "Lorekeeper" of the College of Winterhold can point you in the direction of the Scroll.
- If you have already obtained the Elder Scroll during Discerning the Transmundane, or if you have already completed the *Dawnguard* questline, as soon as The Throat of the World is completed, this quest will be automatically completed as well and Alduin's Bane will begin. Either way, this will skip some of Paarthurnax's optional dialogue.
- If you have the *Dawnguard* add-on installed, the Elder Scroll will now appear as "Elder Scroll (Dragon)" in your inventory.

## Bugs

- This quest occasionally conflicts with the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") quest line. For example, if you are doing the quest [Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment"), [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") will simply say, "we should never have brought that thing here" (referring to the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus")). Urag gro-Shub will sometimes lack the dialogue options required to continue Elder Knowledge. At other times he may not even talk to you, or not place all the books on the desk.
  - This can be resolved by either going directly to Septimus Signus and speaking with him, or by finishing the College of Winterhold quests.
  -  Alternatively, PC users can use the console to progress by advancing to stage 80 (`setstage MQ205 80`).
- If you leave the Tower of Mzark without collecting the Elder Scroll and complete [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane"), collecting the scroll later will have no effect and this quest will be blocked.

  **Mod Notes**: Once Discerning the Transmundane is complete, the reference to "ElderScroll" in DA04ElderScrollActivatorScript is no longer valid, breaking the script.

  - If this happens, the Scroll will not appear in your inventory after collection.
  -  This can be resolved by collecting the Scroll and then spawning it in your inventory with `player.additem 2d513 1`. You should be able to read the Scroll after using this console code.
- The optional quest objective to talk to Esbern may not be listed in your journal.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- You may not be able to start this quest if you have removed the Elder Scroll from your inventory before meeting Paarthurnax. **?**
  -  This can be resolved by using `setstage MQ206 10` to start Alduin's Bane.
- If you don't take the Elder Scroll during [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane") and eventually go on to end that quest without doing so, it becomes impossible to take the scroll later due to the activator being set for an alias in said quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.4, addresses this issue. The activator is instead set to use the alias in this quest to get the scroll since Elder Knowledge is a background quest that is never terminated during the life of the game.

| Elder Knowledge (MQ205) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

If I can recover that same Elder Scroll, I may be able to use it to learn the "Dragonrend" Shout directly from the ancient heroes. *Objective 10:* Learn the location of the Elder Scroll |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* (Optional) Talk to Esbern |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* *or* (Optional) Talk to Arngeir |
| 50 |  | I met the master of the Greybeards, the dragon Paarthurnax. He told me that the ancient Nords used an Elder Scroll to cast Alduin forward in time. If I can recover that same Elder Scroll, I may be able to use it to learn the "Dragonrend" Shout directly from the ancient heroes. Esbern suggested that someone at the College of Winterhold might know how to find this Elder Scroll. |
|  | I met the master of the Greybeards, the dragon Paarthurnax. He told me that the ancient Nords used an Elder Scroll to cast Alduin forward in time. If I can recover that same Elder Scroll, I may be able to use it to learn the "Dragonrend" Shout directly from the ancient heroes. Arngeir suggested that someone at the College of Winterhold might know how to find this Elder Scroll. |
