If I can recover that same Elder Scroll, I may be able to use it to learn the "Dragonrend" Shout directly from the ancient heroes. I've learned that a scholar named Septimus Signus might know where to find it. |
| 80 |  | *Objective 50:* Recover the Elder Scroll |
| 100 | ☑ | I met the master of the Greybeards, the dragon Paarthurnax. He told me that the ancient Nords used an Elder Scroll to cast Alduin forward in time. Now that I've recovered that Elder Scroll, I may be able to use it to learn the "Dragonrend" Shout directly from the ancient heroes. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 40, 45.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ205 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ205`.

Elder Othreloth

**Elder Othreloth**, a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer"), is a priest living in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") and keeper of his town's [Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple").

Previously an [Ashlander](/wiki/Lore:Ashlanders "Lore:Ashlanders"), Othreloth serves as Elder of the Reclamations and advocates the worship of [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura"), [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"), and [Mephala](/wiki/Lore:Mephala "Lore:Mephala") as the "[True Tribunal](/wiki/Lore:New_Temple "Lore:New Temple")". He refers to [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia"), [Sotha Sil](/wiki/Lore:Sotha_Sil "Lore:Sotha Sil"), and [Vivec](/wiki/Lore:Vivec "Lore:Vivec") as false prophets, who misled the people of Morrowind with their "hearts and actions." His beliefs however are not widely accepted by all residents of Raven Rock, as [Aphia Velothi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aphia_Velothi "Skyrim:Aphia Velothi") was banned from the temple for disagreeing with the temple's official stance on the matter.

Like his Apprentice [Galdrus Hlervu](/wiki/Skyrim:Galdrus_Hlervu "Skyrim:Galdrus Hlervu"), he sleeps in the basement of the Temple, in the western chamber, every night between midnight and 7am. At all other times he stands idle in the temple, doing nothing but greeting new visitors.

He wears the [robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Priest_Robes "Skyrim:Temple Priest Robes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Priest_Boots "Skyrim:Temple Priest Boots") of a temple priest. He wields an [elven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger") and carries the [temple key](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Temple_Key "Skyrim:Raven Rock Temple Key") and an assortment of [middle-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). Elder Othreloth knows the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Conjure Familiar").

## Related Quests

- **[Clean Sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:Clean_Sweep "Skyrim:Clean Sweep")**: Clear the [Temple Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Temple Ancestral Tomb") of [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn").

### Dragonborn

:   **Do you know someone called Miraak?**
:   *"Hmm. Sounds like something from a dream, and yet it might be more. Strange."*
:   **What sort of dream?**
:   *"I remember a temple on Solstheim, and working to build something. It... it was not a pleasant dream."*

### Clean Sweep

Othreloth can be questioned about the Ancestral Tombs below the temple, which eventually leads to him to asking you to help deal with the Ash Spawn that have appeared there:

:   **What are the Ancestral Tombs?**
:   *"They are where we inter our dead. They are sacred places, meant to honor their passing. Sadly, we've been unable to use the Ancestral Tomb beneath the Temple as of late, and have resorted to other locations to scatter the remains."*

:   **Why can't you use the tomb?**
:   *"Those foul vermin... the abominations we call ash spawn have risen from the ashes of our own ancestors. They're befouling the memories of our forefathers by defiling their remains."*

:   :   **I'll cleanse the tomb for you.**
    :   *"Thank you, wanderer. That would be most kind. Here, this key should open the door to the tomb."*

:   :   **Well, good luck with that.**
    :   *"Yes, indeed."*

Once the tomb has been cleansed:

:   **The Temple's tomb has been cleansed.**
:   *"Spirits be praised! I'm hoping you didn't suffer much at the hands of those foul beings. Please, accept this as a token of my thanks."*

## Dialogue

At any time, Othreloth can be questioned about some of the details surrounding the True Tribunal and Dunmer burial:

:   **What exactly are the "Reclamations?"**
:   *"The Reclamations are the True Tribunal... the daedra that consecrate the Dunmer people: Azura, Mephala and Boethia. We call them the True Tribunal because they have reclaimed their place in our hearts from the false Tribunal that came before."*

:   **The false Tribunal?**
:   *"Sotha Sil, Almalexia and Vivec represent what was... beings who won the Dunmer people's hearts with their actions, but blinded them just the same. They were aberrations, false prophets. They used their status as heroes to shield the True Tribunal from our minds. But now that they've been destroyed, the light can finally shine upon the House of Reclamations."*

:   **How do the Dunmer bury their dead?**
:   *"The Dunmer race doesn't bury their dead, or leave them to rot inside a stone sarcophagus. When a Dunmer passes, his body is given to fire, so he might return to the ash from whence*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *he came. The Dunmer don't believe that death is the end, we believe that it's the beginning."*

At other times, he may also say:

:   *"Though our spirits may be low, and danger lurks beyond the light, I am confident that They will never abandon us again."*
:   *"May Azura, Mephala and Boethia guide you."*
:   *"Are you here to pray, or perhaps pay your respects at our Ancestral Tomb?"*
:   *"You honor the Reclamations with your actions. This will not be forgotten."*
:   *"The Reclamations herald the dawn of a new age, and the downfall of the false Tribunal."*
:   *"If you're in need of anything material, Attendant Hlervu can assist you."*

## Conversations

At various point throughout the day, Othreloth will converse with his apprentice, Galdrus:

*"Elder, why have the Reclamations destroyed the Tribunal?"*

**Galdrus**: *"Elder, why have the Reclamations destroyed the Tribunal?"*
**Othreloth**: *"The Tribunal's destruction was wrought by their own hands. Their actions, or lack of action caused their downfall."*
**Galdrus**: *"And the Reclamations, they did nothing? Why did they allow the Tribunal to gain our people's favor at all?"*
**Othreloth**: *"Remember your lessons, Attendant."*
**Galdrus**: *""The road to true belief is strewn with the incredulity of those that failed the journey.""*

**Othreloth**: *"Attendant, why has the door to the lower level been locked?"*
**Galdrus**: *"Locked? Are you certain, Elder?"*
**Othreloth**: *"Of course I'm certain. I wished to bless the tombs with the monthly invocation, but I couldn't get the door to open."*
**Galdrus**: *"I'm certain it's only stuck, Elder. I'll speak to Glover Mallory and see if he can take a look at it."*

**Galdrus**: *"You were one of the Ashlanders, Elder?"*
**Othreloth**: *"I was. I wandered the wastes of Vvardenfell, carrying the message of the Reclamations from tribe to tribe."*
**Galdrus**: *"Don't you mean the Anticipations?"*
**Othreloth**: *"We no longer use that name for them. They have reclaimed their identity and no longer represent the patronage of the false Tribunal. You'd do well to remember that next time, Attendant."*
**Galdrus**: *"Of course, Elder. Please forgive me."*

**Othreloth**: *"Galdrus, it's time for your lesson."*
**Galdrus**: *"Very well. I'm ready, Elder."*
**Othreloth**: *"Who are the Reclamations?"*
**Galdrus**: *"The Reclaimations*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *are Azura, Mephala and Boethia. They mean to reclaim what was lost from the Tribunal's falsehoods and lies."*
**Othreloth**: *"Who were the perpetrators of those falsehoods?"*
**Galdrus**: *"Sotha Sil, Almalexia and Vivec. Saints who were never meant to be the cornerstones of our faith."*
**Othreloth**: *"What consequences did we suffer from this fallacy?"*
**Galdrus**: *"The destruction of our homeland, the exile of our people and the rebuilding of our civilization."*
**Othreloth**: *"Why do we rejoice that The Tribunal has fallen and their false promises are but a memory?"*
**Galdrus**: *"We rejoice as the New Temple rises. We rejoice because we embrace the Reclamations as our saviors."*
**Othreloth**: *"Very good, Galdrus. Your lessons are going well. You may carry on."*

## Notes

- He was supposed to be able to have a conversation with [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth"), but since Elder Othreloth never leaves the temple, the two can never meet and the following conversation cannot be heard:

:   **Othreloth**: *"Captain Veleth, I haven't seen you or your men visiting the Temple."*
:   **Veleth**: *"Elder, we barely have enough men to keep the town safe as it is. I can't pull them off watch."*
:   **Othreloth**: *"Our faith is being judged every day, captain. We can't ignore it."*
:   **Veleth**: *"Faith's just going to have to wait, Elder. I'm sorry."*

# Skyrim:Elder

## Overview

Tolfdir, a typical elder

**Elders** (known as **Old People Race** in the game data) is the race that is used for elderly humans in the game. Since Skyrim does not use an "age slider" during the character generation, the elderly are implemented as their own race, but are still treated as other races in-game. Elders gain no skill bonuses for their race, and have no "racial powers", like the Frost Resistance or Battle Cry abilities Nords possess.

## Elders

There are a total of fifty-three elders; forty-six are in the original game. The [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") [add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons") added two more elders, while the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") expansion added four. The [Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate") and [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creations](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") both add one elder.

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit") they are counted as a separate race, similar to how vampires and [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") are treated.
- It is likely that the majority of them are intended to be [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") (based on names, family relations, and the general dominance of Nords in Skyrim), but this is speculative and cannot be confirmed in many cases. At least a few of them are known to be [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") or [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton"). No other races are represented in the elder race.
- There is an additional elder named [Sulvar the Steady](/wiki/Skyrim:Sulvar_the_Steady "Skyrim:Sulvar the Steady") that only appears in the game data. He was related to Windhelm's Wheelhouse, which was removed from the final game.

# Skyrim:Elder

## Overview

Tolfdir, a typical elder

**Elders** (known as **Old People Race** in the game data) is the race that is used for elderly humans in the game. Since Skyrim does not use an "age slider" during the character generation, the elderly are implemented as their own race, but are still treated as other races in-game. Elders gain no skill bonuses for their race, and have no "racial powers", like the Frost Resistance or Battle Cry abilities Nords possess.

## Elders

There are a total of fifty-three elders; forty-six are in the original game. The [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") [add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons") added two more elders, while the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") expansion added four. The [Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate") and [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creations](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") both add one elder.

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit") they are counted as a separate race, similar to how [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") and [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") are treated.
- It is likely that the majority of them are intended to be [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") (based on names, family relations, and the general dominance of Nords in Skyrim), but this is speculative and cannot be confirmed in many cases. At least a few of them are known to be [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") or [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton"). No other races are represented in the elder race.
- There is an additional elder named [Sulvar the Steady](/wiki/Skyrim:Sulvar_the_Steady "Skyrim:Sulvar the Steady") that only appears in the game data. He was related to Windhelm's Wheelhouse, which was removed from the final game.

# Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

Eldergleam Sanctuary

**Eldergleam Sanctuary** is a small [underground grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") and worship site of the followers of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth") south-southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). It contains only one zone, *[Eldergleam Sanctuary](#Eldergleam_Sanctuary)*.

Eldergleam Sanctuary interior

The Eldergleam tree

The sanctuary is renowned for its remarkable beauty and the giant tree [Eldergleam](/wiki/Lore:Eldergleam "Lore:Eldergleam"), which is said to move its roots for [one weapon only](/wiki/Skyrim:Nettlebane "Skyrim:Nettlebane"). The naturally-lit cave also abounds with plants and insects that can be harvested for [alchemical ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, [spadefish](/wiki/Skyrim:Spadefish "Skyrim:Spadefish") can be found swimming in the deeper water.

## Related Quests

- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

### Exterior

The sanctuary is north of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") among the sulphurous pools and hot springs of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch").

### Eldergleam Sanctuary

[Asta](/wiki/Skyrim:Asta "Skyrim:Asta") and [Sond](/wiki/Skyrim:Sond_(bandit) "Skyrim:Sond (bandit)") worship inside. Just before encountering Asta, you will find a chest and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") next to a tree atop the rocks near the northern wall. If you want to mine the corundum, do so before going up to Eldergleam, as [Maurice Jondrelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Maurice_Jondrelle "Skyrim:Maurice Jondrelle") will permanently occupy the vein once his part in the quest is complete. You can also mine it after by attacking the ore with the pickaxe equipped. A copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, v 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v_2 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v 2")* is leaning on the rock next to Asta's knapsack.

A chest protected by Eldergleam's roots is in the back along the western wall. Hit the roots with Nettlebane to access the chest, which contains a random weapon or piece of armor and other loot.

The cave contains the following harvestable ingredients: four [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), two [creep clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), six [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), twenty [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"), three [Jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), and two [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella").

## Notes

- A second corundum ore vein is outside, west of the entrance. Go past the mammoth skeleton and look for it on the other side of the nearby geyser.
- A hunter's camp is outside, southwest of the entrance. At the camp, three "naked" hunters appear to be relaxing in the volcanic hot waters of the shallow pond. Among their possessions is a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") skill book *[Cherim's Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Cherim%27s_Heart "Skyrim:Cherim's Heart")*. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=112691&y=-24574&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- A copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")* and various soul gems are outside, east of the entrance on a crate atop a hill. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=124040&y=-22819&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- Asta's knapsack and all of the items surrounding it are marked as owned by her. Everything else can be taken for free.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary&action=edit).*

Eldersblood Peak

**Eldersblood Peak** is a mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Disarm](/wiki/Skyrim:Disarm "Skyrim:Disarm") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

To reach Eldersblood Peak from the north, go a short distance west on the main road south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") and look for a dirt path to the left. The long path winds past an [unmarked hunter's camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Hunter.27s_Camps "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") and [North Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:North Cold Rock Pass"). To approach the peak from the east, climb a slope northwest of [Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage"), bypassing the enemies on the dirt path.

Before the [dragons' return](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), three [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") (and occasionally some [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider")) will guard the word wall. One frost troll occupies the lowest level, and the other two are near the word wall on the highest level.

After the dragons' return, there will be a dead frost troll on the lowest level. A burned corpse surrounded by scorch marks is on the second level, next to the table. In front of the wall is a dead [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") and another dead frost troll. The third frost troll has been spared by the dragon and will continue to patrol the path below, attacking you if you attempt to approach from the direction of North Cold Rock Pass. The leveled [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") is usually resting on the wall, but the skeletons near [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast") can enter the dragon's detection area, causing it to fly off to investigate.

Regardless of whether [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") has been completed, on the second level there is a sacrificial table with two leveled potions. To the left of the third level is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") plant. The boss chest is to the right of the word wall, between the word wall and the brick wall.

## Bugs

- The word wall may glow or play its sound effect but not give you its word of power. Reloading a previous save or quitting and relaunching the game should resolve the issue. Striking the wall with a spell and pressing against the wall may also work.
- The dragon may not spawn for bounty quests. **?**

# Skyrim:Elenwen

## Overview

Elenwen

Elenwen talking to Malborn

**Elenwen** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [sorceress](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatSorcerer "Skyrim:CombatSorcerer") and First Emissary of the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") in Skyrim. She resides in the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy"), in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") hold. She often hosts lavish parties at the embassy, inviting Skyrim's most influential and powerful people. You infiltrate one of these parties during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), using an ill-gotten invitation.

Elenwen wears [Thalmor robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Robes "Skyrim:Thalmor Robes"), [Thalmor gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Gloves "Skyrim:Thalmor Gloves"), and [Thalmor boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Boots "Skyrim:Thalmor Boots"). She wields a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), which can be up to [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger") in quality. She knows a number of spells, namely [Stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Stoneflesh"), [Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Chain Lightning"), [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), [Ice Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Storm "Skyrim:Ice Storm"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing"), and [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward").

### Main Quest

- **[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")**: Escape [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") custody and a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack.
- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").

### Unbound

Elenwen is introduced in the opening sequence of the game during the wagon ride into Helgen. She can be seen just inside the entrance to Helgen with her bodyguards talking with General Tullius, much to Ralof's dismay:

:   **Ralof**: *"Look at him. General Tullius the Military Governor. And it looks like the Thalmor are with him. Damn elves. I bet they had something to do with this."*

### Diplomatic Immunity

When entering the Thalmor embassy, Elenwen will approach, suspicious of this unknown guest, and will greet you. You will be able to respond with one of three dialogue options:

:   *"Welcome. I don't believe we've met. I am Elenwen, the Thalmor Ambassador to Skyrim. And you are...?"*
:   **My name is <Alias=Player>. Pleased to meet you.**

    :   *"Ah yes. I remember your name from the guest list. Please, tell me more about yourself. What brings you to this... to Skyrim?"*
:   **Quite a party. It's my first time, you know. Where can I get a drink?**

    :   *"Don't worry, my parties are always well-stocked with the finest food and drink available in this country. But first, you were introducing yourself. Please, tell me more about yourself. What brings you to this... to Skyrim?"*
:   **You're Elenwen? I've heard so much about you!**

    :   *"Have you? All good, I trust. But you have me at a disadvantage. I'm afraid I know nothing about you... Please, tell me more about yourself. What brings you to this... to Skyrim?"*

At this point Malborn will interrupt the conversation.

*"Madame Ambassador, I'm so sorry to interrupt..."*

:   **Malborn**: *"Madame Ambassador, I'm so sorry to interrupt..."*
:   **Elenwen**: *"What is it, Malborn?"*
:   **Malborn**: *"It's just that we've run out of the Alto wine. Do I have your permission to uncork the Arenthia red..."*
:   **Elenwen**: *"Of course. I've told you before not to bother me with such trifles."*
:   **Malborn**: *"Yes, Madame Ambassador."*

After this, if you speak to Elenwen again, she may greet you with one of the following lines:

:   *"I trust that this is just the beginning of a long and mutually beneficial relationship."*
:   *"I'm so glad you could attend today."*
:   *"I hope you're enjoying yourself."*
:   *"Please, help yourself to more wine."*
:   *"The hospitality of the Thalmor Embassy is at your service."*

You can also ask her any of the following topics from below:

:   **What's your position on the civil war?**

    :   *"As long as the Empire continues to uphold its treaty obligations, my government does not concern itself with the internal politics of Skyrim."*
:   **I can see you spared no expense**

    :   *"Of course not. One does not gather the most important men and women of Skyrim and then serve them cheap ale and stale bread. This is only a taste of the benefits that accrue to those that align themselves with Thalmor interests."*
:   **I've never quite understood exactly what the Justiciars do**

    :   *"The Thalmor Justiciars are so often misunderstood. Our primary goal is to preserve the peace between the Empire and the Aldmeri Dominion. The worship of the false god Talos contributed to the unfortunate friction that led to the Great War. Following the Great War, the White-Gold Concordat set out the terms for peaceful coexistence between the two powers. The Empire and the Dominion agreed that the worship of Talos was a relic of the past, and must be eliminated in the interests of peace. But I'm sure you didn't come here for a lecture on high politics."*
:   **Do you host these parties often?**

    :   *"Quite often, yes. The only thing I enjoy more than luxury is sharing that luxury with those who can appreciate it. But I also enjoy learning the latest gossip and hear*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *the most intriguing rumors."*
:   **What does your position as Thalmor Ambassador involve?**

    :   *"One of my main duties is to foster a better understanding between the Aldmeri Dominion and the people of Skyrim. I also oversee the activities of the Thalmor Justiciars throughout Skyrim, although this has been unfortunately disrupted by the war."*

### Season Unending

During Season Unending, she is part of the Imperial delegation—along with [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius"), [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") and the Jarl [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")—that attends the Peace Council at [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"). At the start of the council she will say that she has every right to be at this negotiation because she needs to ensure that nothing is agreed to that violates the terms of the [White-Gold Concordat](/wiki/Lore:White-Gold_Concordat "Lore:White-Gold Concordat"). [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") vehemently objects to having a Thalmor representative at the table, and will demand that she leave, though it will be up to you to decide whether she stays or not. Letting her stay makes the Imperials happier with the overall truce, but causes [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") to nearly storm out. On the other hand, her departure makes the Stormcloaks happier, but angers Legate Rikke. Other than this incident, she has no real role in the negotiations.

If you speak to her before taking your seat at the Greybeard's council table, in addition to her standard dialogue, she will also recognize you as the infiltrator from the Embassy, and will say, rather ominously:

:   *"And so we meet again. But this time I know who and what you really are."*

Shortly after Ulfric Stormcloak gets angry due to Elenwen's presence at the peace council, she will stand up for her right to be there:

:   *"I have every right to be at this negotiation. I need to ensure that nothing is agreed to here that violates the terms of the White-Gold Concordat."*

Either General Tullius or Ulfric (depending on your chosen side in the Civil War) will then ask you if she should leave or stay. If you decide she must leave, Elenwen will get up from her seat and say:

:   *"Very well, Ulfric. Enjoy your petty victory. The Thalmor will treat with whatever government rules Skyrim. We would not think of interfering in your civil war."*

After this final line of dialogue for this choice is uttered, she will leave High Hrothgar.

The rest of her dialogue at High Hrothgar is only heard if you choose to let her stay. Ulfric states that she must not participate in the negotiation, but only listen. After Elenwen hears this, she will say to Ulfric:

:   *"Ulfric, why so hostile? After all, it's not the Thalmor that's burning your farms and killing your sons."*

This causes [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") to question whose side she is on. Shortly after this, Esbern will give a speech, which Elenwen will comment on:

:   *"A very pretty speech, but what does it have to do with..."*

Elenwen will then be cut off halfway through the sentence, either by Ulfric saying *"Shut up."* or Tullius saying *"That's enough out of you."*, depending on which of them is getting the short end of the stick in the negotiations.

## Dialogue

In casual conversation, she will mention several subjects, such as her duties as First Emissary. She will speak of the White-Gold Concordat, too, and also mentions her perspective on Tiber Septim and his godhood. She indicates Imperial sympathies in the war, but will deny affiliation in any other dialogue. Since she was at Helgen, she could also mention recognizing you at any time.

:   *"My duty is simple - oversee the Thalmor Justiciars, and make sure they perform their duties admirably."*

:   *"The Empire, in its wisdom, has come to recognize Talos worship as a barbaric remnant of a bygone age."*

:   *"Talos was a heroic man, but not a god. It pains the Altmer that we must remind our younger cousins of the difference."*

:   *"We only want what is best for Tamriel. Surely, the rebels will accept peace when they realize this."*

:   *"I could swear I've seen you somewhere before..."*

### Unused Dialogue

During the quest Unbound, General Tullius appears to have a conversation with Elenwen when he enters Helgen, but they do not actually speak. Unused voice lines exist in the English version of the game, but only for Elenwen, while Tullius's unused lines can be found in the German version. Found below is a rough approximation of how the scene would've played out in-game, with Tullius's dialogue translated to English. The subtitles don't actually exist in the game files, so they were made from scratch and, as such, might not appear punctuated 100% like the developers had envisioned.

:   **Elenwen:** *"General Tullius, stop! By the authority of the Thalmor, I'm taking custody of these prisoners."*
:   **Tullius:** *"Ambassador Elenwen. I guessed that you wouldn't want to miss an execution."'*
:   **Tullius:** *"Do you know my guest, Ulfric Stormcloak, Jarl of Windhelm, once a candidate to Skyrim's throne, traitor of the Empire?"*
:   **Tullius:** *"If you want Ulfric alive, you'll have to take him by force!"*
:   **Elenwen:** *"You're making a terrible mistake..."*
:   **Tullius:** *"I will put an end to this rebellion here and now, rightfully in my position as Legion General."*
:   **Elenwen:** *"Your Emperor will hear of this. By the terms of the White-Gold Concordat, I operate with full Imperial authority!"*
:   **Tullius:** *"All right, let's go."*

## Notes

- She is [voiced](/wiki/Skyrim:Voice_Actors "Skyrim:Voice Actors") by [Jean Gilpin](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jean_Gilpin "wikipedia:Jean Gilpin").
- Elenwen is no longer [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") after you reached Stage 50 of [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") or completed [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). However, you cannot start either of those quests before you complete Diplomatic Immunity, and once that quest is complete she stays in the foyer of the Thalmor Embassy where the party took place, never stepping outside. The problem is that all of the outside doors are unpickably locked, so you can't get back in without using exploits (see [Thalmor Embassy § Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy#Notes "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy")).
- Although not directly involved in the quest, Elenwen also plays a part in [Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute"), as the one who sends [Agent Lorcalin](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_Lorcalin "Skyrim:Agent Lorcalin").
- She shares her name with two other NPCs in *[Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Elenwen "Morrowind:Elenwen")* and *[Online](/wiki/Online:Elenwen "Online:Elenwen")*.
- Elenwen also [appears](/wiki/Castles:Elenwen "Castles:Elenwen") in [*Castles*](/wiki/Castles:Castles "Castles:Castles").

## Bugs

- Rarely, she can be seen outside of Helgen right after you exit the cave with Ralof or Hadvar during Unbound. She will act like she has already met you in the Thalmor Embassy. **?**

Elgrim's Elixirs

**Elgrim's Elixirs** is a damp alchemist's shop located on the lower level, by the canal that flows through the center of the city of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). Owned and run by [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim") and his wife [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg"). It is opposite the entrance to [Beggar's Row](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar%27s_Row "Skyrim:Beggar's Row"), near the northern watergate to [Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim") [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary") (Alchemist)  [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg") [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary") (Shopkeeper) |

## Related Quests

- **[Truth Ore Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:Truth_Ore_Consequences "Skyrim:Truth Ore Consequences")**: Retrieve an [ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quest Items") sample from [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar").
- **[Few and Far Between](/wiki/Skyrim:Few_and_Far_Between "Skyrim:Few and Far Between")**: Help [Ingun](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar") restock [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim")'s rare ingredients.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Elgrim's Elixirs

The proprietor [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim") praises its location as ideal for keeping his [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") fresh, but his wife, [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg"), complains that it is merely the only location he could find that they could afford. Elgrim and Hafjorg both sell merchandise, although they share the same [merchant chest](#Standard_Merchandise) and basically the same purse. [Ingun Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar") is also found in the store during the standard opening hours, as she is apprenticed to Elgrim, who is training her to be an alchemist.

Elgrim's counter

Upon entering, the shop counter is in front of you in an L-shape coming out from the end of the partition wall. Hanging above the partition wall are three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, four bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and two bunches of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). Behind the counter are two sets of shelves holding a selection of ingredients, [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") that are [displayed merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise). On the counter are more items that are displayed merchandise, including those hidden inside a stone bowl on the counter or hidden under the counter, along with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), and a copy of *[Nords Arise!](/wiki/Skyrim:Nords_Arise! "Skyrim:Nords Arise!")*. In the southeast corner is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), with a barrel containing ingredients behind it.

There are two chairs with a small table between them in the northwest corner, with a pile of firewood behind. There is a large fireplace in the west wall, with a wall shelf to the left holding a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a pile of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks underneath. In the southwest corner is a crate with a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on top, and a small round wooden table and three chairs in front. On the table is a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), and a bottle of wine. Near the middle of the south wall is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand with food sacks next to it.

The bedroom

Against the back of the partition wall are three barrels, two of which contain food, while the third contains ingredients. On top of one of them is a copy of *[Palla, volume 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Palla,_volume_2 "Skyrim:Palla, volume 2")*. To the right, in the middle of the wall is a double bed coming out from the wall with an end table holding an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") to the right, a wall shelf above holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a dresser at the foot of the bed holding a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the floor. Opposite, against the south wall is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with Ingun's Alchemy Chest (see [notes](#Notes)) to the left, along with a food barrel with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top in the southeast corner. Against the east wall is a crate, with the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") on top and a wardrobe to the left.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Potions**: 1 [Conjurer's Elixir](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer%27s_Elixir "Skyrim:Conjurer's Elixir"), 1 [Deadly Fear Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadly_Fear_Poison "Skyrim:Deadly Fear Poison"), 1 [Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), 1 [Potion of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), 1 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 1 [Potion of Minor Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Plentiful Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), 1 [Potion of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), 1 [Weak Aversion to Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Fire "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Fire"), 1 [Weak Aversion to Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Frost "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Frost"), 1 [Weak Aversion to Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Magic "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Magic"), 1 [Weak Aversion to Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Shock "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Shock"), 1 [Weak Paralysis Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Paralysis Poison"), 2 [Weak Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison") - **Food**: 2 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") - **Ingredients**: 4 bowls of [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), 1 [Charred Skeever Hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), 4 [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), 1 bunch of Elves Ear, 2 bunch of Frost Mirriam, 2 bulbs of Garlic, 2 [Hagraven Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), 1 sample of [Hagraven Feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), 2 bunches of Lavender, 2 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), 1 [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), 1 [Slaughterfish Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), 3 sprig of Snowberries, 2 [Swamp Fungal Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), 1 bunch of Tundra Cotton, 1 bowl of [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") |

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the store's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ~11 | Common Ingredients | Max 15 (15@75%) |
| 1 | Common [Recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes") |  |
| ~8 | Leveled Fortify Skill Potions | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~13 | Leveled Healing Potions | Max 15 (5@100% + 10@75%) |
| ~8 | Leveled Other Potions | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~8 | Leveled Resist Potions | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~8 | Leveled Poisons | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~1 | Poison [Recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes") | Max 1 (1@50%) |
| 1 | [Potion of Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease") |  |
| ~4 | Rare Ingredients | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~1 | Rare [Recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes") | Max 1 (1@50%) |
| 1 | Salt Pile |  |
| ~8 | Uncommon Ingredients | Max 10 (10@75%) |

## Notes

- Completing [Ingun's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar") [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Few_and_Far_Between "Skyrim:Few and Far Between") provides you with the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun%27s_Supply_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Ingun's Supply Chest Key") to her alchemy chest. It also allows you to freely take the contents of several barrels in the store.
- Even if you complete [Truth Ore Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:Truth_Ore_Consequences "Skyrim:Truth Ore Consequences"), taking any of the other items in the store is still considered stealing. In particular, you are unable to freely take any of the alchemy ingredients sitting on the store's shelves and counters. These are available after also investing in the store, however.
- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the left of the entrance door. There are several alchemical ingredients, potions, and poisons found around the store.
- Elgrim's Elixir's is one of very few stores where you can freely enter the private living space without being followed or asked to leave.

## Bugs

- The store is always open for business, even in the middle of the night, and even if the merchants are sleeping. Simply engage in conversation with the merchant, and you will always be able to trade with them.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.

Elgrim

**Elgrim**, an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:VendorApothecary "Skyrim:VendorApothecary"), is the proprietor of his namesake store [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"). He looks after both his wife [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg") and his promising apprentice [Ingun Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar"). Should anything happen to Elgrim, his wife will take over the shop.

Elgrim's daily routine is heavily [bugged](#Bugs) so he will act unlike any other merchant. His shop is open 24 hours a day, regardless of what he's doing, so you will always be able to barter with him. However, Elgrim will sleep between 11am and 6pm and will then eat a one-hour dinner. He will then wander around the shop, at times eating, sleeping, or using the [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). At 2am he takes his lunch, then returns to wandering before it is time for breakfast at 9am. He finishes his routine with an hour of wandering before his bedtime at 11am.

He wears typical merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothing") with [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223d "Skyrim:Clothing") and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223b "Skyrim:Clothing"). He wields a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality at level 20) and carries the [shop key](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs_Key "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs Key"), a spare [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and a selection of [middle-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). Additionally, there is a 75% chance he may carry a random potion, another 75% chance he will carry a random, rare [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and, lastly, a 50% chance he will carry either a [paralysis poison recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis_Poison_Recipe "Skyrim:Paralysis Poison Recipe") or an [invisibility potion recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_Potion_Recipe "Skyrim:Invisibility Potion Recipe"). He also knows a few spells, specifically [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"), [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"), [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward"), and [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh").

## Related Quests

- **[Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love")**: Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
- **[Further Study](/wiki/Skyrim:Further_Study "Skyrim:Further Study")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Collect a fish to help an alchemist experiment with potions. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

When you enter his shop, he lets you know that he's available to serve you:

:   *"I'm kind of busy, but if you need any potions or ingredients, let me know."*
:   *"I'll be over here if you need any potions or ingredients."*

His greetings:

:   *"You here for lessons like Ingun? Or did you wish to buy something?"*
:   *"Do you have any idea how busy I am? My mixture could be burning as we speak!"*
:   *"Take a look at my supplies if you must, but do hurry... I'm not getting any younger you know!"*

Speaking to him:

:   **Do you work alone?**
:   *"Hardly! In fact, I don't know how I get anything done with all of the distractions I have to put up with. My wife Hafjorg, well, she's a necessary evil I suppose. Not a lick of talent when it comes to alchemy, but she keeps me fed. Then there's Ingun Black-Briar. Bright young thing and a worthy apprentice, when she isn't wasting my rare ingredients."*
:   **Why is your shop down here in the canal?**
:   *"The moisture in the air is better for the ingredients. It isn't every day that you get your hands on fresh [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") or [painted troll fat](/wiki/Lore:Painted_Troll_Fat "Lore:Painted Troll Fat"). It also makes it easier to gather water when the canal is right out the front door. Besides, I also prefer the quiet. I didn't open this business for browsing. Come in, buy what you need and get out."*

When you exit a conversation with him:

:   *"Yes, yes... goodbye."*

### Spread the Love

During [Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love"), you can try to give him a [pamphlet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara"), which he will reject.

:   **Here, brother. Blessings of Mara upon you.**
:   *"I have no time for Marla or Mara or whatever her name is... there's work to be done!"*

## Conversations

*"Ingun, you clumsy fool!"*

At random times, the impatient and grumpy Elgrim will have small clashes with both his apprentice and his wife. Occasionally, Ingun will destroy Elgrim's stock of rare ingredients.

:   **Elgrim:** *"Ingun, you clumsy fool! You've tainted our entire supply of Painted Troll Fat. You have no idea how hard that was to get."*
:   **Ingun:** *"I'm sure my mother can compensate you for it."*
:   **Elgrim:** *"I'll draft a letter to [Rythe](/wiki/Lore:Rythe_Lythandas "Lore:Rythe Lythandas"). If you could have it sent to [Cheydinhal](/wiki/Lore:Cheydinhal "Lore:Cheydinhal") for me, that would make up for your blunder."*
:   **Ingun:** *"I'll make sure it's sent right away."*

Sometimes you'll walk in on Ingun asking Elgrim about the contents of her lessons.

:   **Ingun:** *"I don't understand, Elgrim. The formulas you're giving me are for novices but I've advanced well passed*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *that point."*
:   **Elgrim:** *"Until you can do those formulas with your eyes shut, you'll never be ready to master the more difficult ones."*
:   **Ingun:** *"This is an utter waste of time."*
:   **Elgrim:** *"Ingun! If you want to remain in my shop as an apprentice I expect you to act like one. No exceptions!"*
:   **Ingun:** *"Very well, I'll keep practicing them."*

Hafjorg expresses her concerns over Ingun's practices.

:   **Hafjorg:** *"Elgrim, honey. I'm concerned about your new pupil. She seems very... odd."*
:   **Elgrim:** *"Ingun? She's brilliant; a natural!"*
:   **Hafjorg:** *"Oh dear, I didn't mean to say she isn't bright. It's the things she makes here, the things she says and all those poor little animals she tests them on. It's just not right."*
:   **Elgrim:** *"Damn it, woman! Ingun is the most promising alchemist I've ever seen and I won't have you scaring her off!"*

Elgrim might irritably accost his wife over a missing ingredient, which he assumes she moved.

:   **Elgrim:** *"Hafjorg! Where did you put it woman?!"*
:   **Hafjorg:** *"Sigh. What is it now, dear?"*
:   **Elgrim:** *"Don't you "dear" me! I had a bowl of Vampire Dust on my worktable not an hour ago and after you swept in there it's gone!"*
:   **Hafjorg:** *"Oh my. Elgrim, it's on the shelf to the right of the table, as always."*
:   **Elgrim:** *"Ah, I see. Well, just be careful around my things!"*

## Notes

- In a scene with Ingun, Elgrim makes a direct reference to the rarity of [painted troll fat](/wiki/Oblivion:Painted_Troll_Fat "Oblivion:Painted Troll Fat"). Painted troll fat appeared in [Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion") as a very rare alchemy ingredient, limited to a mere six samples in the entire game.
  - He also mentions that he gets this ingredient from "[Rythe](/wiki/Oblivion:Rythe_Lythandas "Oblivion:Rythe Lythandas")" in [Cheydinhal](/wiki/Oblivion:Cheydinhal "Oblivion:Cheydinhal"). Rythe Lythandas also appeared in Oblivion and was related to the [quest](/wiki/Oblivion:A_Brush_with_Death "Oblivion:A Brush with Death") in which you could get the troll fat. Elgrim's dialogue implies that Rythe is still alive and living in the same city over 200 years later.

## Bugs

- Elgrim was clearly meant to go to bed at 11pm, but his bedtime was set to 11am, making him sleep during most of the shop's intended opening hours. Additionally, his lunch package was set to 2am instead of 2pm.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Take Torygg's war horn to the Shrine of Talos.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") |
| Location(s): | [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") |
| Reward: | [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor") available for purchase |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =2 ([Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair")) |
| ID: | SolitudeFreeform07 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf") | **Next →** [Thane of Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf") | | → Next | [Thane of Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar") | | |

Torygg's war horn in place at the Shrine of Talos

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair").
2. Place [Torygg's War Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Torygg%27s_War_Horn "Skyrim:Torygg's War Horn") at the shrine of Talos [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=52654&y=8111&zoom=16&legacy=true).
3. Return to Elisif.

### A Personal Request

After you complete [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf"), [Elisif's](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") goodwill towards you has increased. So much so that she extends a tentative trust in you by making a personal request regarding her late husband, [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"). She will tell you, *"When we buried my husband I made offerings to all the gods... except [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos")."* This is because Talos worship is outlawed in the Empire. She would like you to take [Torygg's War Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Torygg%27s_War_Horn "Skyrim:Torygg's War Horn") and place it at a specific [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines"). Although she doesn't worship Talos herself, her husband would have wanted a proper [Nordic](/wiki/Lore:Nord "Lore:Nord") burial done in this fashion.

### The Shrine of Talos

Travel to the Shrine of Talos in the wilderness of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), due north of [The Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone"). Follow the path near [Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave"), along the northern bank of the river, and you can find the shrine behind some trees. As you approach the shrine, [Agent Lorcalin](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_Lorcalin "Skyrim:Agent Lorcalin") and a [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") soldier will appear and attack you, as Lorcalin is under [orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Lorcalin%27s_Orders "Skyrim:Lorcalin's Orders") from the [Thalmor emissary](/wiki/Skyrim:Elenwen "Skyrim:Elenwen") to kill any Talos worshippers he can find. Once the horn is placed in front of the statue of Talos and the quest updates, you are free to take it away at any time without affecting the quest's progress, and it will no longer be marked as a quest item.

### The Jarl's Good Grace

Return to Elisif at the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") where she will reaffirm her belief in you and allow you to purchase [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor") as well as take the next step to becoming a [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane").

## Notes

- Prior to completing the prerequisite quest, the horn can be pickpocketed from Elisif. It will be marked as a quest item and cannot be removed from your inventory without completing the quest.
- Fighting the Thalmor is not necessary to finish the quest; they can be [calmed](/wiki/Skyrim:Calm "Skyrim:Calm") or evaded in order to activate the statue's base.
- The Thalmor will always spawn the first time you are at the shrine, regardless of whether you're doing the quest.

## Bugs

- The Thalmor may not spawn at all because of a random encounter such as a dragon attack, although this doesn't affect the quest.
- Alternatively, the Thalmor may spawn at the shrine itself, frequently sitting on one of the benches.

## Quest Stages

| Elisif's Tribute (SolitudeFreeform07) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Take Torygg's War Horn to the Shrine of Talos for Elisif the Fair. |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Talk to Elisif |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 30, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage SolitudeFreeform07 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest SolitudeFreeform07`.
