Elynea Mothren

Elynea at her alchemy lab

**Elynea Mothren** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:VendorApothecary "Skyrim:VendorApothecary") and mycologist living in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"). She needs your [assistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House") in repairing the [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") tower and in [acquiring](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_and_Gathering "Skyrim:Hunting and Gathering") certain ingredients for her. Having served [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") for decades, she is frustrated that he would replace her if she does not immediately repair the tower, something she is unable to do due to her old age and reluctance to place herself in danger. According to [Talvas](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon"), she seems to be friendly with Neloth's steward, [Varona Nelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas"), often requesting her to purchase ingredients from [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

She wakes up at 8am to tend her duties as apothecary, closing her shop at 8pm. She goes to bed at 10, but before the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") is [cleansed](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"), she will work there instead of sleeping.

She wears a set of merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots"), and she carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Apothecary_Key "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Apothecary Key") to the [Tel Mithryn Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Apothecary "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Apothecary"), some assorted [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), and gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Healing a House](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House")**: Help Elynea Mothren repair the tower of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").
- **[Hunting and Gathering](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_and_Gathering "Skyrim:Hunting and Gathering")**: Collect a rare alchemy [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") for Elynea Mothren.
- **[Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward")**: Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Further Study](/wiki/Skyrim:Further_Study "Skyrim:Further Study")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Collect a fish to help an alchemist experiment with potions. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

Her greetings:

:   *"Hmmph. Another wanderer. I suppose you'll be wanting potions, just like the others."*
:   *"I like it here at Tel Mithryn. Hardly anyone bothers me. People can be so irritating."*
:   *"You'd think Neloth was still a clan leader in [House Telvanni](/wiki/Lore:House_Telvanni "Lore:House Telvanni") the way he carries on."*
:   *"Mushrooms and molds of [Vvardenfell](/wiki/Lore:Vvardenfell "Lore:Vvardenfell") have adapted to the ash far better than the green plants."*
:   *"It's almost time to feed the mushrooms. They like a drop of blood every now and then you know."*
:   *"It's a shame about Varona."*
:   *"My back still hurts from all that stone work. Why were we at that standing stone anyway?"*

When spoken to:

:   **What do you have for sale?**

    :   *"I've got the best selection of mushroom and fungi."*
    :   *"I probably have some potions around here that might interest you."*
    :   *"Every type of fungus in Solstheim or Skyrim. Oh, and a few other ingredients and potions."*

:   **Did you come here from Morrowind?**
:   *"Yes. That was a lifetime ago. I was just a young girl when [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain") erupted. Master Neloth was already old. My mother put me on a boat to Skyrim. The last time I ever saw her, she was standing on the dock as my ship sailed away."*

:   **What do you do for master Neloth?**
:   *"I am his mycologist. He may have grown Tel Mithryn by himself, but I nurture it. Mushrooms and fungi are my life's work. When I saw Tel Mithryn I knew I had to be here. I've learned so much since then."*
:   **Did you grow this tower?**
:   *"Me? No. That's Master Neloth's doing. I wasn't even born then. It's Telvanni magic at its best. He brought the cuttings with him from Morrowind and used sorcery to grow them."*

If you encounter her at the Sun Stone and cleanse the stone she can be spoken to:

:   *"Who brought me here? They better not have touched my mushrooms. Neloth? Neloth! Is this your doing?"*
:   *"This just isn't right. Why was I working on that stone?"*

Her goodbyes:

:   *"Azura light your steps."*
:   *"Mephala cloak you."*

### Conversations

Elynea and Drovas in conversation

If Varona is alive, Elynea will sometimes talk to her:

**Elynea**: *"Are you going to Raven Rock soon? I need some thing."*
**Varona**: *"Soon. Be patient. Ulves is still making his list. And of course Master Neloth keeps adding to his. What with all the ash spawn on the road these days, I'm not leaving until the trip is worth it."*
**Elynea**: *"Bah! Patience is for the young. An old dunmer like me can't afford it."*

**Varona**: *"I'm sick of all this ash. I know dunmer aren't supposed to mind the ash, but I hate it."*
**Elynea**: *"It's a good thing you've always lived here on Solstheim. Vvardenfell is covered in ash. Red Mountain makes sure of that."*
**Varona**: *"So you've said a hundred times. But didn't you also tell me the Telvanni lands were green and lush?"*
**Elynea**: *"Maybe two hundred years ago they were. Now they say those green lands are ash covered too."*

If Varona is dead, Elynea will instead converse with her replacement [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi"):

**Elynea**: *"I miss Varona. She used to help me with the gardening."*
**Drovas**: *"I can't help it if I have a black thumb. It's like the mushrooms hate me."*
**Elynea**: *"It's not your fault, Drovas. You do other things well. Varona was never able to do the repair work that you do."*
**Drovas**: *"Thank you. I didn't mean to be so defensive. I know Varona was your friend. It's okay to miss her."*

**Drovas**: *"Do you ever get lonely out here in the middle of nowhere?"*
**Elynea**: *"You complain too much. Tel Mithryn is the safest place in Solstheim. Only a fool would challenge Master Neloth."*
**Drovas**: *"I suppose you're right. At least here I'm safe from Mogrul."*

### From the Ashes

While the ash guardian is alive outside she will say:

:   *"Someone should do something about that damned Ash Guardian."*

### Reluctant Steward

When you are [searching](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") for Varona, asking Elynea if she's seen her:

:   **Have you seen Varona?**
:   *"She left for Raven Rock hours ago. She promised to bring me back some fresh blisterwort."*

Later when you inform her of Varona's death:

:   **Varona is dead. I found her body on the road.**
:   *"Dead? Oh, merciful ancestors! That blasted wizard couldn't be bothered to give her some protection for those trips. This is all his fault. Best tell Neloth. I'm sure he'll mourn for all of two seconds."*

### Old Friends

During the quest [Old Friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Friends "Skyrim:Old Friends"), asking Elynea about [Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril"):

:   **What can you tell me about Ildari Sarothril?**
:   *"She was a headstrong one. Always pushing Master Neloth to teach her more. Her lust for power was her undoing. She let Master Neloth do some ritual thing to her. We buried her out back. That was some twenty years ago now."*

### Healing a House

If you have not helped her heal Tel Mithryn, you may hear Elynea complaining about Neloth's treatment of her, saying, *"Damn that man! He is being totally unreasonable."*, *"That ash eating wizard is always on me about his tower. It's not my damn fault the thing withered overnight."*, or *"I don't care if he's a Master Wizard. He can't treat me like this!"* Asking her what Master Neloth did will have her explain the situation:

:   **Master Neloth? What did he do?**
:   *"That fetcher told me to fix his house. If I don't, he'll find a new mycologist who will. Decades of loyal service, and he'd just throw me out like yesterday's breakfast!"*
:   **What do you need to fix the tower?**
:   *"Three taproots soaked in the [headwaters of the Harstrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Headwaters_of_Harstrad "Skyrim:Headwaters of Harstrad") river. I'm an old woman. I can't possibly make that trip. It's way too dangerous. If you get some taproots, I'll pay you to dip them in the headwaters and bring them to me."*

:   :   **Where can I get taproot?**
    :   *"Where do you think? You have to cut it out of a [Spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"). Although sometimes you can buy them from alchemists."*

:   :   **What can you tell me about the Harstrad Headwaters?**
    :   *"It's special to the Spriggans. They seem to like to gather there. Something about the waters attracts them. There are bound to be some there, so be careful."*

Once you have the soaked taproots:

:   **I have the three soaked taproots.**
:   *"Truly? Well done. I'll just keep two of them for myself. No need for Neloth to know. Take that last taproot and plant it into the wall of the withered house."*

Return to her after you've planted the taproot. She will hand you two leveled [potions of well-being](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Well-being "Skyrim:Potion of Well-being") with the words:

:   **The soaked taproot is planted.**
:   *"Good. Now maybe Neloth will get off my back about it. I suppose you think you should get paid for helping an old woman. Here. Take these. I'll sell you more if you come back later."*

### Hunting and Gathering

To start the quest Hunting and Gathering, ask her if she needs help. Her dialogue depends on which ingredient she currently needs:

| Ingredient | Elynea's Reply Before | Your Dialogue | Elynea's Reply After |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") | *"Well, I could use a daedra heart. Can't grow that in my garden."* | **"I've got a daedra heart."** | *"It's a bit dried up, but it will do. Here."* |
| [Giant Toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe") | *"Hmm. I'm running out of giant toes. I'll pay extra for one."* | **"I've got a giant's toe."** | *"A bit ripe, isn't it? Here. Take this."* |
| [Hagraven Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw") | *"As a matter of fact, I need a hagraven claw. I'll pay extra if you find one."* | **"I've found a hagraven claw."** | *"Nasty bitches, aren't they? Here's your fee."* |
| [Vampire Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust") | *"How about some vampire dust? Bring me some of that and I'll pay handsomely."* | **"I've *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* have some vampire dust."** | *"Not bad for an amateur? Take this."* |
| [Briar Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart") | *"You got a briarheart? That's what I really need. Neloth keeps taking all of mine."* | **"I have a briarheart."** | *"You could have cleaned it. It's still bloody. Here's your money."* |
| [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") | *"You find some void salts and you bring them to me. I'll beat anyone else's price."* | **"I have some void salts."** | *"Hmm. Better than average quality. I'll take it."* |

## Notes

- Breaking into Elynea's shop outside of business hours does not count as trespassing, and she will happily trade with you if you wake her up.

## Bugs

- She was supposed to comment on Varona's regular trips: *"Varona goes to Raven Rock all the time. I'm sure she's fine."* during Reluctant Steward, but will not due to a scripting oversight.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

## Overview

Embershard Mine

**Embershard Mine** is a small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") southwest of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains only one zone, *[Embershard Mine](#Embershard_Mine)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Smith 'N Slash](/wiki/Skyrim:Smith_%27N_Slash "Skyrim:Smith 'N Slash")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Defeat an [Orc blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Yakhtu gra-Orkulg") and her bandits to obtain an enchanted set of armor.

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Rescue your beloved from kidnappers.
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)")**: Slay a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") leader for [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

A slightly hidden path leads from the banks of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") to the mine; the path is recognizable by the wooden slats leading up to it. As you approach the mine, a bandit will warn you to stay away, then rush to attack if you linger or continue to approach. A wooden cart, a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood"), and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") are by the barrels outside the entrance, with a beehive above and to the right of the entrance. With *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry") is to the left of the entrance, just beside the wooden cart.

### Embershard Mine

Mine interior

The mine itself is fairly well lit, but a light source will definitely come in handy, so you may want to grab some torches from the torch sconces scattered throughout to dim the area and aid in sneaking and to use for later exploring once the enemies are dispatched. There are ten samples of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") to harvest throughout the mine. As you descend into the mine, there is a [falling log](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap that can do a fair amount of damage if you are low-level. The trigger for the trap is a tripwire across the dirt floor, so hop up onto the boards on the right of the tunnel to avoid the tripwire. The tunnel ends at a wooden walkway that crosses a large, mostly natural chamber. The walkway is suspended well over the ground below which is mostly covered by shallow water. Below this walkway to your right is a small beach where two bandits occupy a campsite with two unowned bedrolls. If you sneak in, you can overhear the two bandits mentioning the guard outside and the trap. If you remain hidden after this discussion, one of the bandits will lie down on a bedroll, and the other will take the ramp from the campsite up to the end of the walkway opposite the entrance and then go through the tunnel on the far side of the chamber to a platform where he will stand, facing the entrance tunnel. There is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") near the campsite's campfire in case you need one to start mining [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"). The tunnel that leads to the platform intersects with a dead-end, collapsed tunnel section where you will find a [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a [tattered journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Tattered_Journal_(Embershard_Mine) "Skyrim:Tattered Journal (Embershard Mine)"). The platform holds a food barrel, a shelving unit, a small table and chair, and a lever which will lower a drawbridge to form a T-intersection with the wooden walkway. If the two bandits from the campsite have been killed, lowering the drawbridge alerts two more bandits who will come to investigate. If you remain hidden, they will split up with one heading for the platform and the other checking the entrance tunnel.

Across the lowered drawbridge is a dark tunnel. Just before the tunnel, a coin purse sits on a beam overhead. It can be snagged manually with a little careful maneuvering, knocked down with an arrow or spell, or, with some luck, you can activate the lever to raise the bridge, and then attempt to cross it as it rises; it will propel you upwards and place you atop the entrance to the dark tunnel. You might want to quicksave before knocking down the coin purse in case it gets lost in the water below. Moving forward into the tunnel, you will pass a partially boarded opening in the right wall. A small opening in the boards acts as a window to a treasure room. Around the corner, a bandit sits on a chair outside the locked door to the treasure room. This bandit carries the [Embershard Mine key](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine_Key "Skyrim:Embershard Mine Key") which opens both the treasure room and the prison cell opposite. The treasure room contains a boss [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), several sacks, a weapon rack that holds an iron greatsword and an iron warhammer, two alchemy barrels, and a small table. A *[Spell Tome: Clairvoyance](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Clairvoyance "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Clairvoyance")*, an iron dagger, and a coin purse sit on top of the table.

Deeper into the mine, the tunnel opens onto a ledge on the eastern wall of an even larger chamber. The eastern ledge holds two alcoves, one of which contains three unowned bedrolls, a small table, and a chair. The other alcove contains nothing but a bucket set into a wooden floor. From this eastern ledge, wooden ramps on the north and south walls lead down to the blacksmith area below, which contains a forge, a grindstone, a workbench, a weapon rack that holds an iron sword and an iron greatsword, and a table. There are two iron ingots on the workbench, and there are two pieces of iron ore and a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Light Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Light Armor Forging")* on the table. A wooden walkway on the south side of the chamber leads to a southern ledge that appears to be the main dining area and pantry. The dining area contains three tables - two with chairs, a shelving unit, a brazier with some grilled leeks and baked potatoes on top, and a couple of sacks. The pantry has some large shelves and contains numerous sacks, two food barrels, a table, and a chest. A coin purse, several loose coins, and a few [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") sit on the table. A tunnel in the west wall of the dining area leads to a smaller ledge with another coin purse and a novice-locked chest nestled next to the waterfall. From the dining area ledge, another suspended wooden walkway spans the chamber to a walkway on the northern wall. This walkway, part earthen and part wood, leads to the highest ledge which is on the west side of the chamber. This area is rigged with bone chimes and has an exit back outside just southwest of Riverwood. There are three more bandits in this chamber. One is working the forge, a two-handed warrior is seated in the dining area, and an archer patrols the suspended wooden walkway and the western ledge with the bone chimes. The bottom floor of the chamber is mostly covered by water. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found here, and fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be caught.

## Notes

- [Iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") are found in the following locations:
  - Next to the first campfire after you first descend into the mine.
  - At the first intersection, between the collapsed tunnel and the bridge lever room.
  - At the bottom of the tunnel just after the bridge, next to a wood pile.
  - Just past the jail cell, behind boards that appear to be supporting the wall.
  - Just past the jail cell, next to a wood pile in the corridor.
  - At the bottom level of the large room, under the walkway between the water and the forge.
  - In the middle level of the large room, next to the waterfall accessed via the path behind the kitchen.
  - On the path from the top level of the large room, next to a bone rattle alarm just before the unmarked exit near Riverwood.
  - In addition to the above eight veins inside the mine, two more are outside the mine, a short distance northwest of the unmarked exit.
- Entering from the unmarked exit may result in the two bandits behind - now in front - of the lever-controlled bridge not spawning. It appears the trigger for the two bandits to spawn is the act of lowering the bridge from the side nearer the main entrance.
- If the two bandits in the first chamber are alive or reanimated when the bridge is lowered, the two bandits that usually spawn and run across it will not spawn.
- Killing the bandit boss clears the mine, but you may wish to avoid this, as it will force a 30-day waiting period for the ore veins to respawn. If you leave the boss alive, you can visit the mines every ten days for more iron ore, making this mine a prolific source of iron ore. Some quests that send you here only require an item to be retrieved, which can still be done without killing the boss, though the target chest is beside the boss.
- Unlike most bandit hideouts, there is no Bandit Chief in this dungeon, even if you have a bounty quest requiring you to kill the leader of the mine. The leader will instead usually be a normal bandit, or on rare occasions, a Bandit Outlaw. This may be due to the fact that this dungeon is one of the few that has a maximum level as well as a minimum level.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, this dungeon is an excellent place to stock up on iron for [housebuilding](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") purposes.

## Maps

- 

  Embershard Mine

Embry in Riverwood

**Embry** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [lumberjack](/wiki/Skyrim:Lumberjack "Skyrim:Lumberjack") and the local drunk of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").

He can always be found in and around the [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") where he is allowed to drink all night long. He starts his day at 7am, taking a one-hour breakfast in the taproom, then heads outside on the porch where he spends the next nine hours loitering around, either sitting on the bench or leaning against the railing. At 5pm he heads back inside and spends the entire evening (and night, due to a [bug](#Bugs)) drinking and dancing.

Embry wears a set of lower-class [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes"), a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"), and a pair of [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"). He carries a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Key to Sleeping Giant Inn") to the inn. He wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

## Related Quests

- **[A Farmer's Life For Me](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Farmer%27s_Life_For_Me "Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming"): Develop your farm.
- **[Quest all Drunks Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Drunks_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Drunks Have")**: Make a drunk dance for joy. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

When approached, he will often respond with a drunken:

:   *"You're kinda fuzzy. What's wrong with ya?"*
:   *"Outta my way, stranger."*

## Conversations

When he spends time on the porch, he will often try to persuade one of the local guards to drink with him:

**Embry**: *"My favorite drinking buddy! Let's get some mead."*
**Whiterun Guard**: *"Not now. If I don't pull night duty, I'll drink a round with you at the Sleeping Giant."*
**Embry**: *"But I'm thirsty now."*
**Whiterun Guard**: *"You're always thirsty. Just like you're always drunk. Now let me get back to my rounds."*

Also, if he meets [Sigrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigrid "Skyrim:Sigrid") he will make a poor attempt at an invitation:

**Embry**: *"Care to have a drink with me, sweet Sigrid?"*
**Sigrid**: *"Drunk again, Embry? Don't let [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor") hear you talking to me that way. He'll stick your head in his forge."*
**Embry**: *"So that's a no I take it?"*

Sometimes, he may ask for some ale from Orgnar:

**Embry**: *"I need some more ale, Orgnar."*
**Orgnar**: *"You've had more than enough. Besides, you still haven't paid for the last one."*
**Embry**: *"I'll find some coin for you. I always do."*
**Orgnar**: *"Until then, I've no ale for you."*

Sometimes, he may ask for a drink from Orgnar using one of the following lines:

**Embry**:

- *"Gimme a mug of ale."*
- *"A pint of your finest mead."*
- *"Some wine, please?"*
- *"I'll have some mead."*
- *"Pour me some ale."*

Orgnar will then reply using one of the two potential lines:

- *"Coming right up."*
- *"Certainly."*

He may also approach [Hod](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod "Skyrim:Hod") to ask him for a drink:

**Embry**: *"How's about a drink, Hod."*
**Hod**: *"You'll be wantin' me to pay for them?"*
**Embry**: *"It's only right seein' as your*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *the important lumber man."*
**Hod**: *"You come do an honest day's work at my mill, and I'll pay you an honest day's wages. Then we'll drink."*

## Bugs

- Embry was supposed to sleep at the inn between midnight and 7am, but he just keeps drinking.

  **Mod Notes**: his radius is way too small to reach any of the available beds

  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- If you pickpocket Embry and fail, he will run into his room and will alternately run around and cower while speaking as if you had defeated him. He will continue cowering even if you attack him. **?**

# Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (decoy)

## Overview

| Emperor Titus Mede II (RefID: 0004bccb) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II "Lore:Emperor Titus Mede II")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | | |
| Location | [Castle Dour, Emperor's Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour,_Emperor%27s_Tower "Skyrim:Castle Dour, Emperor's Tower") | | |
| Race | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Assassin_(class) "Skyrim:Assassin (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0004bccb | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001d4ba |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 1 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") | | |
| Class Details | [CombatAssassin](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatAssassin "Skyrim:CombatAssassin") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | Any Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleCondescending](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [DB09TowerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DB09TowerFaction "Skyrim:DB09TowerFaction") | | |

.jpg)

The Emperor's decoy

**Emperor Titus Mede II** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") acting as a decoy in place of the real [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)"), during the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire"). He was put there by [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro") as part of a conspiracy to rid the Brotherhood of their new Listener, namely you, and will be seated in the dining area of the [Emperor's Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour#Emperor.27s_Tower "Skyrim:Castle Dour") of [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). His real name is never given.

He wears [Emperor's robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Emperor's Robes") and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots").

## Related Quests

- **[To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire")**: Attempt to assassinate the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") while disguised as the [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet "Skyrim:Gourmet").

### To Kill an Empire

Once you have finished the famous Potage le Magnifique, with or without an added pinch of [jarrin root](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarrin_Root "Skyrim:Jarrin Root"), you are to follow fellow chef [Gianna](/wiki/Skyrim:Gianna "Skyrim:Gianna") up the stairs to the dining area. As you approach the door, you will overhear a conversation between the Emperor, a [Nobleman](/wiki/Skyrim:Nobleman "Skyrim:Nobleman"), and a [Noblewoman](/wiki/Skyrim:Noblewoman "Skyrim:Noblewoman"):

**Noblewoman**: *"But aren't even you the least bit nervous? After everything that's happened?"*
**Titus**: *"You mean the wedding? My cousin's apparent murder? An unfortunate misunderstanding, no more. Cold mead, hot tempers... these things happen."*
**Nobleman**: *"Quite. Yet that recent business with the young officer. Maro, was it? How dreadful. The son of your commander, plotting your assassination."*
**Titus**: *"Yes, an unfortunate turn of events, that. But an isolated incident. And I have been assured that the fault was with the man's son alone. Truth is, we are in no danger whatsoever. Killing an Emperor can be useful, but befriending one? Now that's beneficial - as I'm sure you'd all agree."*

At this point, he will look up and say:

:   *"Aha! Here we are. Honored guests, I present to you - the Gourmet! Ah, the Potage le Magnifique. So delicious. My friends, as Emperor, I of course reserve the right of first taste."*

While the guests laugh, it is possible to speak to Titus, who will say:

:   *"I've been waiting for this opportunity for a long time."*
:   *"So glad we kept you in Skyrim. Serving your Emperor was worth the wait, of course."*
:   *"You're not at all what I expected. I imagined you'd be fatter, honestly."*
:   *"You've done your duty and we're all very grateful. Now... I'd like to eat."*

The Emperor will taste the soup and his next line depends on whether or not you poisoned the dish. If it is okay, he will say:

:   *"Oh... Oh how marvelous. Just delicious. It is everything I had hoped it would be. Please, everyone. Enjoy."*

He will then just keep eating until you take action.

If the soup is poisoned his reaction will be less pleasing:

:   *"Oh... Oh how marvelous. Just delicious. It is everything I had hoped it would be. It.... I.... I think something's... wrong... I..."*

He will then drop dead in his seat.

## Notes

- This decoy Emperor is identical to the real Emperor in every way except voice.

# Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)

## Overview

| Emperor Titus Mede II (RefID: 0004FA39) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II "Lore:Emperor Titus Mede II")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah") | | |
| Race | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Assassin_(class) "Skyrim:Assassin (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0004FA39 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001D4B9 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 1 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") | | |
| Class Details | [CombatAssassin](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatAssassin "Skyrim:CombatAssassin") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [Unique](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-Unique "Category:Skyrim-Voice-Unique") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionHaafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar "Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar"); [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction") | | |

Emperor Titus Mede II

**Emperor Titus Mede II** is the current Emperor of [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel") at the time [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") takes place. He is an aged, wise and powerful man, who is forced into visiting Skyrim by the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), upon the command of [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre"). After successfully dodging an assassination attempt from the Dark Brotherhood through the deployment of a decoy, he was finally found on his ship, [The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah"), near Solitude docks departing from Skyrim. When you enter his cabin, Mede seems to have accepted his fate, but he asks you to kill the man who ordered his death.

Titus Mede II's reign includes the Great War and the signing the White-Gold Concordat ending the war. He is also a talented tactician, and was an integral part of defeating the occupying Thalmor forces in the [Battle of the Red Ring](/wiki/Lore:Great_War "Lore:Great War").

He wears a set of [Emperor's robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Emperor's Robes") along with a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000cee82 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He carries a [Katariah master key](/wiki/Skyrim:Katariah_Master_Key "Skyrim:Katariah Master Key").

## Related Quests

- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest contracts in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.

### Hail Sithis

Upon entering his chamber in the Katariah, even if you are invisible or sneaking, he will acknowledge you by saying:

:   *"And, once more, I prove [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro") the fool. I told him you can't stop the Dark Brotherhood. Never could."*

He will then initiate conversation with you, saying:

:   *"Come now, don't be shy. You haven't come this far just to stand there gawking."*

You now have three dialogue options with the Emperor:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **You were... expecting me?** | *"But of course. You and I have a date with destiny. But so it is with assassins and emperors, hmm? Yes, I must die. And you must deliver the blow. It is simply the way it is. But I wonder... would you suffer an old man a few more words before the deed is done?"* |
| **Your rule is at an end! Sithis commands it!** | *"Oh, you can save your sinister bravado. I'll not go to my grave whimpering like an infant. I know why you're here. I must die. And you must deliver the blow. It is simply the way it is. But I wonder... would you suffer an old man a few more words before the deed is done?"* |
| **(Remain Silent)** | *"You and I have a date with destiny, it would seem. But so it is with assassins and emperors, hmm? Yes, I must die. And you must deliver the blow. It is simply the way it is. But I wonder... would you suffer an old man a few more words before the deed is done?"* |

Any of the three dialogue options lead to the following three more dialogue options with the Emperor:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **I'm listening.** | *"I thank you for your courtesy. You will kill me, and I have accepted that fate. But regardless of your path through life, I sense in you a certain... ambition. So I ask of you a favor. An old man's dying wish. While there are many who would see me dead, there is one who set the machine in motion. This person, whomever he or she may be, must be punished for their treachery. Once you have been rewarded for my assassination, I want you to kill the very person who ordered it. Would you do me this kindness?"* |
| **I've heard enough. Your life ends now.** | *"Tsk. How unfortunate. I had hoped you would honor an old man's dying wish. Well, let's be done with it then."* |
| **(Remain Silent)** | *"You will hear me out, then? Good. You will kill me, and I have accepted that fate. But regardless of your path through life, I sense in you a certain... ambition. So I ask of you a favor. An old man's dying wish. While there are many who would see me dead, there is one who set the machine in motion. This person, whomever he or she may be, must be punished for their treachery. Once you have been rewarded for my assassination, I want you to kill the very person who ordered it. Would you do me this kindness?"* |

Telling him you've heard enough will make him exit conversation with you making your only choice then to kill him. The other two dialogue options will result in the next three dialogue options being available:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **I'll... consider your request.** | *"Thank you. Now, on to the business at hand I suppose, hmm?"* |
| **A Dark Brotherhood assassin doesn't do... favors.** | *"Hmph. Pity. I had hoped to obtain even a modicum of justice. Well, on to the business at hand then, hmm?"* |
| **(Remain Silent)** | *"Well. Perhaps you'll at least consider it, hmm? Now, on to the business at hand..."* |

All three of the dialogue options above make the Emperor exit conversation with you. Talking to the Emperor after he has exited conversation with you will only result in him saying:

:   *"Well? I won't fight you, so we may as well get this over with."*

## Notes

- Somewhat ironically, Titus Mede II's class is [assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatAssassin "Skyrim:CombatAssassin").
- He is voiced by [Wes Johnson](/wiki/General:Wes_Johnson "General:Wes Johnson"), who voiced the male Imperials in [Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion").
- Even if you are an Imperial Legion member, killing Emperor Titus Mede II has no effect on the progression of the Imperial storyline.
  - However, if you join the Imperial Legion after killing the Emperor, [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") will omit his name from the oath he administers to induct you into the legion.
- Titus, as well as the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus"), will still remain in Skyrim even if you've resolved the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") in favor of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), even though Skyrim is supposed to be an independent nation at that point. However, it is unlikely the Emperor would openly recognize their independence in this case, and was still forced to come to Skyrim by his cousin's murder.
- The Penitus Oculatus will continue its presence in the game, even after you kill the Emperor, despite the fact that you can overhear Commander Maro saying otherwise before killing him.
- During [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire"), Titus sends an almost identical [decoy](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(decoy) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (decoy)") to Solitude in his stead.
- He is the author of the *[Letter to General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_General_Tullius "Skyrim:Letter to General Tullius")* added by the [Lord's Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club").
- Emperor Titus Mede II also [appears](/wiki/Legends:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II "Legends:Emperor Titus Mede II") in the [Heroes of Skyrim](/wiki/Legends:Heroes_of_Skyrim "Legends:Heroes of Skyrim") card expansion for *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*.

## Bugs

- If you get a cinematic kill when attacking him, he might die at the beginning of it (such as before an arrow/bolt hits him, or a melee weapon makes contact), rather than at the end of the animation. **?**

# Skyrim:Enchanting Pick-Up

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **[Sergius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") wants you to pick up an item from a client for enchanting.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") |
| Location(s): | Various |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| ID: | MGR10 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") | | |

Sergius Turrianus in his room at the College of Winterhold

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").
2. Collect the item he wants.
3. Return to Sergius.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Sergius will request that you pick up an item to be enchanted from a customer, located somewhere in Skyrim. The NPC will be in a city, won't be part of either the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") or the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"), and will have one of the following voicetypes: [FemaleElfHaughty](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleElfHaughty "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleElfHaughty"), [FemaleDarkElf](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleDarkElf "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleDarkElf"), [FemaleEvenToned](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleEvenToned "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleEvenToned"), [MaleElfHaughty](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleElfHaughty "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleElfHaughty"), [MaleDarkElf](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDarkElf "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDarkElf"), or [MaleEvenToned](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenToned "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenToned"). Most of the possible NPCs are elves, but not all. In total, there are 57 possible NPCs. Locate the NPC and speak with them to obtain the item required, which will be a piece of [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"). Return to Sergius to complete the quest and be rewarded. You will be rewarded with a leveled amount of gold for the delivery of the item.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- After the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quest [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers"), [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar") may stay in [Calcelmo's Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo%27s_Tower "Skyrim:Calcelmo's Tower") and not leave. In this case, the dialogue option to accept the item from him will not be available. If you try and pickpocket him, he is not carrying the item. He is immediately hostile towards you, and you will receive a bounty in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") as a guard will come to your location. Attacking and killing [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar") fails the mini-quest.
  - After killing [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar") and returning to [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") you can continue to receive his radiant quests as normal.
- It is possible for Aicantar to randomly return to his original routine in Understone Keep after completing Hard Answers when receiving this quest; if this happens, receiving the Enchantment Pick-Up quest can force him to remain there for the duration of the game, or simply reappear at Calcelmo's Tower.

## Bugs

- You may be directed to an NPC who is already dead (i.e. killed by a vampire if you have the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on installed), making the quest impossible to be completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Enchanting Pick-Up (MGR10) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Sergius Turrianus needs an item picked up from <Alias.ShortName=Client> in <Alias=ClientLocation> and returned to him so that he can enchant it. *Objective 10:* Go to <Alias.ShortName=Client> in <Alias=ClientLocation> and pick up the item |
| 20 |  | I've received the item from <Alias.ShortName=Client> and need to deliver it to Sergius at the College so he can enchant it. *Objective 20:* Return the item to Sergius Turrianus |
| 200 | ☑ | I've finished the task that Sergius gave me, and have successfully picked up and delivered the item from <Alias.ShortName=Client> so that it can be enchanted. |
| 255 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGR10 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGR10`.

# Skyrim:Enchanting Tutorial

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Use an [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") |
| Location(s): | [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | TutorialEnchanting |

Enchant your items

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Use the [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") in [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"), with [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire")'s guidance.

### A Student of the Craft

On top of his duties as court wizard, [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") also provides tips on the basics of [enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") to prospective mages. Find him at his research station in [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") and ask him how to enchant weapons and armor. Upon doing so, he will introduce you the basics of enchanting in Skyrim:

*"Ah, a student of the craft. You'll need to start by learning an [enchantment](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Effects "Skyrim:Enchanting Effects"). Take an enchanted weapon or piece of armor, then use the Arcane Enchanter to learn its secrets. The item is destroyed in the process, so be wary. Once you know an enchantment, you'll need a filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and something to enchant. You'll use the Arcane Enchanter for that, too. Of course I have everything you need for sale, if you have the coin."'*

### Master in the Making

Using this advice, you may walk over to his arcane enchanter and begin enchanting. The quest will complete upon activating the enchanter. It is not necessary to enchant or even disenchant an item to complete this quest.

## Notes

- This quest will end with no failure message if you stray too far from Dragonsreach, either by fast travel or by simply walking down the steps outside. The quest remains active throughout nearly all of Dragonsreach including both the Great Porch and the castle grounds, but can disappear if you get too close to the secret escape to the Guard Barracks in the dungeons.[*verification needed*]
- This quest is always available, even if you already have 100 Enchanting levels.

## Quest Stages

| Enchanting Tutorial (TutorialEnchanting) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Use the Arcane Enchanter |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TutorialEnchanting stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TutorialEnchanting`.

# Skyrim:End of the Line

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Collect resources to help [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") set up her own market stall.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") delivers [Letter from Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Viriya "Skyrim:Letter from Viriya") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | [Viriya's Charm](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya%27s_Charm "Skyrim:Viriya's Charm") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Crab\_MQ3 |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Wave Breaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Wave_Breaker "Skyrim:Wave Breaker") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Wave Breaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Wave_Breaker "Skyrim:Wave Breaker") | | |

Help Viriya build her dream stall

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the letter from Viriya.
2. Obtain 18 pieces of firewood, 20 nails, 4 iron fittings and a lock.
3. Bring the building supplies to Viriya
4. Wait 24 hours.
5. Visit Viriya's stall in the Grand Plaza.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Soon after completion of [Wave Breaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Wave_Breaker "Skyrim:Wave Breaker"), a courier will deliver you yet another [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Viriya "Skyrim:Letter from Viriya"). It's from Viriya. In her hiatus, she has decided to leave the Riften Fishery and run a Mudcrab merchant stall within the Riften "Grand Plaza." The objective is to bring her building materials for the stall. She needs: 18 pieces of Firewood, 20 Nails, 4 Iron Fittings and a Lock. Bring all the gathered items to her:

:   **Here's everything you'll need to build a stall in the plaza.**
:   *"By the Gods. I don't even know what to say."*
:   **I'll stop by the plaza tomorrow once you've gotten everything set up.**

Wait for 24 hours. After that time goes by visit her new market stall in the Plaza. She'll thank you for helping her with her dream job and will commence to give you an enchanted amulet named [Viriya's Charm](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya%27s_Charm "Skyrim:Viriya's Charm"):

:   **Look's like you're all set up.**
:   *"It would seem so. I wanted to give you this, a token of my appreciation. Thanks, good luck out there."*

This ends the Fishing questline. Fishing radiant quests can still be done for [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water") afterwards. These include the quests for: [Further Study](/wiki/Skyrim:Further_Study "Skyrim:Further Study"), [Rubbish Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Rubbish_Retrieval "Skyrim:Rubbish Retrieval") and [Stocking Up](/wiki/Skyrim:Stocking_Up "Skyrim:Stocking Up").

## Notes

- Once Viriya becomes a merchant, she will have 150 gold. You cannot invest with her, but her shop benefits from the [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader") perk.

## Quest Stages

| End of the Line (ccBGSSSE001\_Crab\_MQ3) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've received a letter from Viriya. I should read what it has to say. *Objective 10:* Read the letter from Viriya |
| 20 |  | Viriya is planning to leave the Riften Fishery and start her own market stall in the Grand Plaza specializing in her passion, mudcrab. I should see if I can help her by obtaining all of the supplies she will need to build her stall so she can move on to her next venture. *Objective 0:* Obtain 18 pieces of firewood  *Objective 1:* Obtain 20 nails  *Objective 2:* Obtain 4 iron fittings  *Objective 3:* Obtain a lock  *Objective 20:* Bring the building supplies to Viriya |
| 40 |  | I have given Viriya everything she needs in order to build her own market stall in the Grand Plaza. I should wait for her to set it up. *Objective 30:* Wait 24 hours for Viriya to set up her market stall |
| 55 |  | Viriya should have her market stall in the Grand Plaza set up by now. I should pay her a visit when I have the chance. *Objective 40:* Speak to Viriya |
| 200 | ☑ | I spoke to Viriya at her new market stall, where she has started a new chapter in her life beyond the Riften Fishery. I'm glad she was able to realize her dream of farming and selling mudcrab meat. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 25, 50.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Crab_MQ3 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Crab_MQ3`.

Endarie

**Endarie** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [tailor](/wiki/Skyrim:Tailor "Skyrim:Tailor") living in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). She runs [Radiant Raiment](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment") along with her twin sister [Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie"), and she can be found behind the counter in the store while Radiant Raiment is open. Endarie's personality is not very welcoming, and she is frequently rude to you. If you invest in her shop, however, her [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you will increase.

She sleeps from midnight to 8am, then wakes up to work in Radiant Raiment. At 8pm she closes the store and spends the rest of the day relaxing around the store.

Endarie wears a set of merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006ff45 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries the [key to the store](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Radiant_Raiments "Skyrim:Key to Radiant Raiments") and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When you approach her, she may greet you with:

:   *"Oh, what delight. Another charming customer..."*
:   *"Let me just drop everything to help you. I don't mind. Really."*
:   *"I can help with purchases, but if you came to talk, see my sister. She's the one who gets on with people. It's her one virtue, really."*
:   *"So good to see you again. How can I be of service?"*

Speaking to her, if you have completed [Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!"), [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames"), or [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened"), or have invested in her business, will change her dialogue:

:   **Do you get a lot of business like that?**

:   :   *"Radiant Raiment has the finest attire in all of Skyrim. That is how we get business."*

:   :   *"I suppose I would, but you're the only one who gets that greeting."*

:   :   *"Oh, we do all right. Rumor is, you had a hand in the Blackblood Marauders' demise... I'm impressed."*

:   :   *"Radiant Raiment has the finest attire in all of Skyrim. That is how we... Wait. You're that new bard, the one who saved the Festival. Aren't you? That was a good bit of work."*

:   :   *"It's never been an issue. People say you helped with the problems at Wolfskull Cave. I applaud anyone who assists the court."*

Her dialogue will also change depending on your disposition with her:

:   **Bad day?**

    :   *"You'd think so, wouldn't you? I'm fine. Thank you for asking."*

:   :   *"It is when my customers waste time chatting, and not buying."*

:   **You seem to be in a good mood.**
:   *"Only when you're around. The rest of these fools I could do without."*

Her goodbyes:

:   *"Finally..."*
:   *"Thank the gods for the end of yet another pointless conversation..."*

## Conversations

:   **Taarie**: *"Sister dear, could you try sewing those sleeves a little tighter? We can't have our customers looking sloppy because of your work."*
:   **Endarie**: *"Oh certainly, dear sister. We couldn't afford to have our customers look like the simple pigs they are, now could we?"*
:   **Taarie**: *"Good. And while you're at it, perhaps you should sew your mouth shut when our fine customers are within earshot, hrm?"*

[Irnskar Ironhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irnskar_Ironhand "Skyrim:Irnskar Ironhand") may also talk with [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") about a new gown by Endarie:

:   **Irnskar**: *"My lady, I'm pleased to inform you that you have a new gown for court, specially tailored by madame Endarie."*
:   **Bryling**: *"Really? How did we afford that? Besides, I like the gown I already have."*
:   **Irnskar**: *"Madame Endarie insisted. She made it free of charge, in honor of your lenience about last month's rent discrepancies."*
:   **Bryling**: *"That was suspiciously nice of her. I thought she hated everyone."*
:   **Irnskar**: *"She does, my lady. But apparently, she hates you just a little less than the others."*

## Notes

- Endarie has the exact same facial data as her sister, [Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie").
  - The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* states that the two are twin sisters, so it's possible they're meant to be identical twins.

## Bugs

- One of Endarie's responses after you finish [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened") is incorrectly set to play after completing [Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!") instead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

Endon's House

**Endon's House** is the home of [Endon](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon"), [Adara](/wiki/Skyrim:Adara "Skyrim:Adara"), and [Kerah](/wiki/Skyrim:Kerah "Skyrim:Kerah") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

It is next door to the Treasury House, on the first terrace up, above the abandoned house.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Adara](/wiki/Skyrim:Adara "Skyrim:Adara")  [Endon](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon") [Fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Fence") \*  [Kerah](/wiki/Skyrim:Kerah "Skyrim:Kerah") [Jeweler](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Jeweler") |

\* Only becomes a fence after completing the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining").

## Related Quests

- **[Silver Lining](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining")**: Recover a stolen [silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold") for a [silversmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Endon's House

The entrance is normally adept-locked. The property has piles of fancy cookware throughout including [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), [platters](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") and [jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), etc. Upon entering there is a large room with a couple of shoulder-height partition walls segregating separate areas. On your right against the east wall is a set of shelves holding a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and a copy of *[Chaurus Pie: A Recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Pie:_A_Recipe "Skyrim:Chaurus Pie: A Recipe")*, with a barrel containing bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") to the right, in the corner and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots") on the floor beside it. Further along the wall to the left is a small square table and chair with a [silver amethyst ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Amethyst_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Amethyst Ring") on top and a washbasin to the left, with a bowl on top, containing an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"). There is a food barrel in front of the partition wall to the north.

In the southwest corner of the room is a small raised area with a long stone table against the west wall with two display cabinets on top, they are both adept-locked and contain many different [silver necklaces](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace") and [rings](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring"). To the left, against the south wall is a set of shelves holding an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). To the right of the stone table is a small set of shelves with a food barrel to the right of them. In the northwestern corner is a door through into a bedroom, while in the northeastern corner is another raised section. This one has a fireplace on the east wall with a piece of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") in the flames. To the left is an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), with a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") along the west wall. Against the back of the partition wall is a stone table with a piece of silver ore and an open crate containing four [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") on the table and another open crate to the left of the table, on the floor holding five pieces of silver ore.

Through the door into the bedroom there is a wooden bench and stool on the left, against the west wall, with a plate of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese on top of the stool and a bowl of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") on the floor. To the right, against the south wall is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand and against the east wall is a long wooden table with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), a portion of grilled leeks, two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") and a cast iron pot containing a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). Under the table is a basket containing a cabbage, a gourd and two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato").

To the north is a raised section with two small flights of stairs up to it, with a low wall between them holding a platter and gourd. In the center of the north wall is a king-sized bed coming out from the wall with an end table to the right, on top of which is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"). In the northeastern corner, along the east wall is a child's single owned bed, with a round wooden table and chair at the foot of the bed with a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") and a copy of the non-skill book version of *[Vernaccus and Bourlor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vernaccus_and_Bourlor "Skyrim:Vernaccus and Bourlor")* on top. To the left of the king-sized bed is a dresser with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [blue butterfly wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing") and a [silver sapphire necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Sapphire_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Sapphire Necklace") on top. Against the west wall is a set of shelves holding a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a couple of pieces of cheese, a [slaughterfish egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs and a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust").

Pac-man?

## Notes

- In the far side of the house there are samples of garlic, glow dust, sliced goat cheese, and a slaughterfish egg which clearly resemble [Pac-man](/wiki/Skyrim:Easter_Eggs#Pac-Man "Skyrim:Easter Eggs").
- There are two [shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") found here:
  - A  "Fence") Fence shadowmark is to the left of the entrance door. This is due to the fact that after you complete the [reputation quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining") in Markarth, [Endon](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon") becomes a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)") for you and the guild.
  - A  "Protected") Protected shadowmark is to the bottom left of the door because Endon is a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

# Skyrim:Endon

## Overview
