Endon

**Endon** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") who is usually in the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). He is the husband of the merchant [Kerah](/wiki/Skyrim:Kerah "Skyrim:Kerah") and the father of [Adara](/wiki/Skyrim:Adara "Skyrim:Adara"). He is often seen in the company of his daughter perhaps hinting that the two are close. Conversations between Endon and his family indicate that he also has a son, Cade, who has left Markarth to join up with the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

Prior to completing [Silver Lining](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining"), his [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon%27s_House "Skyrim:Endon's House") is locked and he wanders the streets of Markarth when he is not in the inn. After the quest is complete, he becomes a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)") and can be found either in his home or wandering randomly around town (most often either in the plaza in front of the inn or on the stone bridge overlooking it).

Endon does not feel that his family is safe in Markarth and the attack in the marketplace only confirms his fears. After the attack he can be heard arguing with his wife Kerah. She wishes to stay in the city but Endon feels that it isn't safe and wants them to move elsewhere. However, any plans Endon might have to move his family out of Markarth are never acted upon and he can always be found within the city walls.

Endon wears a set of merchant's [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothes") along with a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#0004223b "Skyrim:Hat") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots"). He carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Endon%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Endon's House") to his house, [Kerah's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Kerah%27s_Key "Skyrim:Kerah's Key"), and a selection of [upper-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). In combat, he relies on an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

## Related Quests

- **[Silver Lining](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining")**: Recover a stolen [silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold") for a silversmith.

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Endon's [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"), once Endon becomes a [Fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | Leveled [Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") | Enchanted |
| ~10 | [Lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") | Max 14 (6@100% + 4@75% +4@25%) |

## Dialogue

His greetings:

:   *"I work silver, like my father, and his father before him."*
:   *"My wife Kerah runs our jewelry stall in the market."*
:   *"My daughter Adara is also my apprentice. She's a quick study."*
:   *"I prefer working in silver. More skill needed than forging iron or steel."*

When ending conversation:

:   *"I have silver to bend."*
:   *"Farewell."*

### Fence Dialogue

As fence, he will receive some new business-related greetings:

:   *"Glad your*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *here, I've been looking for some more merchandise to buy. Have lots of orders to fill and my clients don't like to wait."*
:   *"Now I know you've come by for more than just a visit. What did you bring?"*
:   *"I promise you, I buy much more than simple silver trinkets."*
:   *"I've made a lot of new contacts thanks to you, and more contacts means more coin for everyone."*
:   *"I've been forbidden to deal with you until amends are made with the Guild. Sorry."* **(If Guild rule has been broken)**

When spoken to:

:   **How's business?**
:   *"Business is absolutely booming, my friend. I've taken to hiring a few extra men of my own just to keep up with all the shipments. Old Delvin certainly takes care of his own, doesn't he."*

:   **What'll you give me for these?**
:   *"Usual guild rate. Let's take a look at them."*

After fencing some goods, he will end the conversation by saying

:   *"When you get back to Riften, tell Delvin this new arrangement's working out quite well."*

### Conversations

After the [incident](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") at the marketplace, Endon goes to talk to his distraught wife, obviously concerned with her safety:

:   **Kerah**: *"What am I supposed to do? Never leave the house? You want that, Endon?"*
:   **Endon**: *"You're closing the stall, and that's final."*
:   **Kerah**: *"You want to give up now? Out of fear? Is that what we're teaching our daughter?"*
:   **Adara**: *"Mama, why are you and papa fighting?"*
:   **Endon**: *"We're not fighting we're just.... Why don't I get you something to eat? Mama and papa will talk later."*

While Kerah is at her stall, Endon might come over to chat:

:   **Kerah**: *"Hello, dear husband. Have you brought more silver jewelry for me to sell?"*
:   **Endon**: *"Yes, I have. Adara made the rings herself. She is learning to bend the metal well."*
:   **Kerah**: *"They are perfect. Thank you both."*

:   **Endon**: *"How are the necklaces selling, my wife? We could make more."*
:   **Kerah**: *"I'm afraid the necklaces aren't selling well. Customers are not interested in medallions engraved with the symbols of other provinces."*
:   **Endon**: *"Humph. Used to be everyone in Markarth wore a necklace showing his home province, from Elsweyr to High Rock to Hammerfell and Cyrodiil..."*
:   **Kerah**: *"We don't have travelers from Elsweyr or Hammerfell anymore, Endon. Only the natives and the [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") stay in Markarth now."*
:   **Endon**: *"As they always have, along with those crazed [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). They've driven off the color that used to make this city great."*
:   **Kerah**: *"I need to get back to the customers. We'll talk more of this when I come home tonight."*

Endon may be seen having random conversations with his family in [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn"):

:   **Kerah**: *"What should we have tonight?"*
:   **Endon**: *"Something simple, a stew perhaps."*
:   **Adara**: *"Stew again, papa? I want steak."*
:   **Kerah**: *"Maybe we could spend a little bit more and buy some meat, Endon."*
:   **Endon**: *"May be. Let me think about it."*

*"Markarth has changed, but the inn is as lively as ever."*

:   **Endon**: *"Markarth has changed, but the inn is as lively as ever."*
:   **Kerah**: *"The city hasn't changed that much, dear. Some old dwarven stones gathering the same old moss."*
:   **Endon**: *"The stones aren't what bother me, love. The Forsworn are tearing the Reach apart."*
:   **Kerah**: *"Let's not talk about this over dinner."*

At home, Endon and his family may have more conversations:

:   **Adara**: *"Mama, when is Cade coming home?"*
:   **Kerah**: *"He's off fighting, Adara, with the Stormcloaks. He'll return when the war is over."*
:   **Endon**: *"Our son joining the Stormcloaks. If this war had never happened, Cade would have joined the Imperial Legion, like grandfather."*
:   **Kerah**: *"Endon, we talked about this... Are you still disappointed in Cade's choice?"*
:   **Endon**: *"No. I think if I was a young man, I would have done the same."*
:   **Adara**: *"Can I join the Legion when I grow up?"*
:   **Endon**: *"If there's still a Legion left, Adara. I'm sure you'd make a great soldier. Just like your brother."*

:   **Kerah**: *"We sold all those lovely little necklaces you brought me today. Did you make them yourself?"*
:   **Adara**: *"That's right! Papa helped me with the clasps, but I did all the links on my own."*
:   **Endon**: *"Adara bends the silver so naturally. Grandmother would have cried if she saw how deft our daughter has become."*
:   **Kerah**: *"Well, I'm proud of both of you. I haven't been so busy since those nobles from [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") come into the city three years ago."*
:   **Endon**: *"I miss those days, before the Forsworn took up arms again, when you could walk the roads in peace."*
:   **Kerah**: *"Endon, dear, please don't.... Save your frustrations for work."*
:   **Endon**: *"You're right, dear. I'm sorry to worry you."*

### Silver Lining

When you are ready to perform the [special assignment](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining") for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in Markarth, you can go and speak to Endon:

:   **Delvin Mallory sent me.**
:   *"Oh thank goodness! I wasn't sure where else to turn..."*
:   **Just start from the beginning.**
:   *"Several months ago I ordered a [special silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold") from some artisans in Valenwood by way of a Khajiit Caravan. Well, it never arrived. Later I found out that it was robbed by a group of bandits led by someone named [Rigel Strong-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Rigel_Strong-Arm "Skyrim:Rigel Strong-Arm")."*
:   **Why do you need the Guild's help for that?**
:   *"Look, I talked to the Jarl, the Steward, the Housecarl... everyone. They all told me their resources were spread too thin right now. Word on the street says that the Thieves Guild is coming back into its own in Markarth so I figured..."*
:   **Send a thief to steal back what was stolen.**
:   *"Exactly. Look, this mold is irreplaceable. I'll pay you well for its return and I can also prove to be quite a valuable ally to the Thieves Guild."*
:   **No time to lose then.**
:   *"Yes, indeed. The only thing I can tell you is that the mold was taken to the bandit's hideout... a small cottage called [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"). I'm not sure how many men they have inside, but I trust that won't be an issue for you. Good luck."*

When you either return from Pinewatch with the mold or already have it in your inventory when receiving the quest, Endon will be very content with you and the Guild:

:   **I have your silver mold.**
:   *"You've more than proven that the Thieves Guild is back on its feet in our city and earned every bit of your reward. Tell Delvin that he can count on me to provide the influence around here with the right people when he needs it. If you're ever looking to sell any illegally obtained merchandise, I'd also provide my services as a fence. It's the least I can do."*

## Notes

- Endon's fence inventory may always have 4 of the same kind of enchanted jewelry for sale.

# Skyrim:Endrast

## Overview

| Endrast (RefID: 000F03F2) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Alftand Animonculory](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand") | | |
| Race | [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Sorcerer](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorcerer "Skyrim:Sorcerer") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000F03F2 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0003B0E4 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| Class Details | [CombatSorcerer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatSorcerer "Skyrim:CombatSorcerer") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions_C#College_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Factions C") (Scholar); [CrimeFactionWinterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionWinterhold "Skyrim:CrimeFactionWinterhold") | | |

Endrast

**Endrast**, a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") [sorcerer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatSorcerer "Skyrim:CombatSorcerer"), was a local explorer of some renown who accompanied [Sulla Trebatius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sulla_Trebatius "Skyrim:Sulla Trebatius") on an expedition to the [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand") Dwemer ruins.

After they were captured by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), he managed to pick the lock on their cell so they could escape. Despite initially being saved by [Yag gra-Gortwog](/wiki/Skyrim:Yag_gra-Gortwog "Skyrim:Yag gra-Gortwog"), he succumbed to his wounds beneath Dwarven steam pipes in the animonculory not long after writing his final thoughts in his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Endrast%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Endrast's Journal"), found nearby his corpse along with a piece of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), and a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick").

Endrast wears [ragged robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Robes "Skyrim:Ragged Robes") with no shoes.

## Notes

- Endrast was likely created with [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir") as a base, as he still retains some of the latter's AI packages and factions. This also results in a number of oddities, as seen below.
  - At some point, the Unofficial Patch also removed the AI packages from his package list, although this isn't noted in the changelog.

## Bugs

- He's part of the College of Winterhold faction, despite never being found there. This inclusion could lead to his death triggering the [Rejoining the College](/wiki/Skyrim:Rejoining_the_College "Skyrim:Rejoining the College") quest should he be [reanimated](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate_(spells) "Skyrim:Reanimate (spells)") and re-killed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=21011))
- Due to the fact that he's part of the [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") crime faction, should you resurrect and re-kill him, then you could theoretically receive a bounty in that hold.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.

Engar

**Engar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") and a [carriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#Carriage "Skyrim:Transport") driver who can be hired at [Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor").

He wields an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), and wears farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006C1D8 "Skyrim:Clothes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0003452f "Skyrim:Boots").

## Related Quests

- **[Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find and rescue [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").
- **[Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): The time of prophecy has arrived! Locate [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") for the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").

## Notes

- There is an unnamed [Stormcloak soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") referred to as Engar by [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist#The_Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") during the quest [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)").

## Bugs

- Engar is mistakenly set as part of CrimeFactionFalkreath rather than CrimeFactionHjaalmarch.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Enmon's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Enmon's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Enmon%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| KarthwastenEnmonsHouse | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Enmon's House

**Enmon's House** is a two-story residence in the southwestern part of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"), located between [Karthwasten Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten_Hall "Skyrim:Karthwasten Hall") and [Miner's Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Karthwasten Miner's Barracks").

It is the home of [Enmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon "Skyrim:Enmon") and his wife [Mena](/wiki/Skyrim:Mena "Skyrim:Mena"). It consists of one zone, *[Enmon's House](#Enmon.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Enmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon "Skyrim:Enmon")  [Mena](/wiki/Skyrim:Mena "Skyrim:Mena") |

## Exterior

| Plants | Mushrooms |
| --- | --- |
| 2 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  1 [Juniper Berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") | 1 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita")  3 [White Cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") |

## Enmon's House

Ground floor

The ground floor is used as the kitchen, dining, and storage area of the home. A non-respawning dresser immediately to the right of the door holds three [potions of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina") and two [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). A respawning food barrel sits in the northwest corner, with a well stocked set of shelves to its left which holds a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), and two bottles each of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on the top shelf, while the middle shelf holds three [eidar cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") and three [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), and the bottom shelf holds a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and six [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). To the left of these shelves is a non-respawning cupboard holding three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on the top shelf and one bottle each of wine and alto wine below. Sitting before the cupboard and shelves is a dining table set with three loaves of bread, two [goat cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), three bottles of alto wine, and two servings of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat").

On the southern wall, some hanging foodstuffs can be found on the right side, including two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, some dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), and two portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). The fireplace is situated to the left, with two bottles of Nord mead on the mantel and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") at its base. Hanging to the left above the fireplace are four freshly caught [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). A small round table near the fireplace holds a goat cheese wedge, a bottle of Nord mead, a loaf of bread, and a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). Towards the southeast corner, beneath the stairs, a set of shelves holds three [silver ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") on the top shelf, an additional pickaxe and five [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") on the middle shelf, and a copy of the book *[Nords Arise!](/wiki/Skyrim:Nords_Arise! "Skyrim:Nords Arise!")* along with three pairs of miner [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000e3445 "Skyrim:Boots") on the bottom shelf. A respawning food barrel sits on each side of the base of the stairs.

Upstairs

Going upstairs will lead to the bedroom area of the home. Along the south wall, a set of shelves can be found holding an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and various kitchenware. Directly ahead, on the western wall, is a double bed (belonging to the [KarthwastenEnmonsHouseFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:KarthwastenEnmonsHouseFaction "Skyrim:KarthwastenEnmonsHouseFaction")) with a small non-respawning chest resting at its foot. A small table to the right holds five gold coins, and a non-respawning dresser to the left holds three bottles of Nord mead and a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe"). A door leads to the balcony of the house on the north wall, and a single square table with a chair is situated just to the right of it.

## Notes

- The front door and balcony door both have a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Enmon%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Enmon's House") to which is carried by both Enmon and Mena.
- The balcony, which is accessible through the upstairs area of the home, hosts a bench which holds two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine").
- During [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella"), the doors to Enmon's House will lock if night falls while inside it. Unlocking the door at this point is considered a crime. Waiting until morning causes the door to unlock.

Enmon

**Enmon** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") living in [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") with his wife [Mena](/wiki/Skyrim:Mena "Skyrim:Mena"). They have a daughter named [Fjotra](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra"), who has been kidnapped by a group of [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").

As it turns out, Fjotra is the new sybil of Dibella, and you will be directed to travel to Karthwasten and speak to Enmon. When you tell him of your intention to liberate the girl from her Forsworn captors, he will insist on accompanying you. However, he can be talked out of it if you prefer to travel alone. He contributes very little to the battle and is likely to be killed in the rescue attempt, so the best decision may be to leave him in Karthwasten.

He wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00080699 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and is equipped with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). He carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Enmon%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Enmon's House") to [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon%27s_House "Skyrim:Enmon's House") and a selection of [lower-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").

## Dialogue

:   *"You're not from here, and we don't need to be talking."*
:   *"You should talk to [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach"). He's in charge."*
:   *"Don't have nothing to say to you, stranger."*
:   *"Karthwasten doesn't need outsiders prying in our business."*

After completing [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella"):

:   *"I hope Fjotra is happy in the temple. We're so honored to have given her."*
:   *"Thank you for getting her back from the Forsworn. Dibella was smart to have sent you."*

## Quest-Related Dialogue

:   **I'm looking for a young girl who lives around here.**
:   *"Damn it, man/woman, are you trying to taunt us?"*

    :   **What are you talking about?**
    :   *"Our daughter, Fjotra, was taken from here. The [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") descended and... they didn't touch anything else. Just our little girl."*

        :   **Where did they take her?**
        :   *"It was the Forsworn from [Broken Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt"). Never been much trouble before. What's it to you?"*

            :   **Your daughter is the Sybil of Dibella.**
            :   *"She... really? That's... I wouldn't have dreamed. Of course, we need her in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), then. I'll come with you."*

                :   **We'll save her together.**
                :   *"Thank you, friend."*
                :   **It's dangerous out there. You should stay.**
                :   *"You're... probably right. Just hurry, please. Who knows what those things are doing to her."*
            :   **I just want her to be safe.**
            :   *"That's... that's good of you. If you were to save her, I would be very grateful. I don't think there's anything I could give you, though..."*

If he follows you, he may say the following as you progress the quest:

:   *"Let's get to the Forsworn camp. Her life could be in danger."*
:   *"I swear, if those things have laid a hand on her..."*
:   *"Let's find Fjotra. This place gives me the creeps."*
:   *"How could they live like this? It's disgusting."*

After fighting through the dungeon and reuniting with his daughter:

:   **I've found your daughter.**
:   *"Fjotra!"*

:   **[Fjotra](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra"):** *"Father!"*
:   **Enmon:** *"Fjotra, dear. Did they hurt you?"*
:   **Fjotra:** *"Of course not. My spirit remains strong."*
:   **Enmon:** *"My little girl. Always strong. Do you know where you have to go?"*
:   **Fjotra:** *"I'm to go to the [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella") in Markarth. I... I'll have to leave you and mother."*
:   **Enmon:** *"It's our honor to have you there. This man/woman is going to take you to Markarth. Are you ready?"*
:   **Fjotra:** *"Of course."*

## Conversations

:   **Enmon:** *"When are those [Silver-Blood men](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Mercenary "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Mercenary") going to leave?"*
:   **[Belchimac](/wiki/Skyrim:Belchimac "Skyrim:Belchimac"):** *"Never. They've shut us down forever, Enmon. The [Divines](/wiki/Lore:Nine_Divines "Lore:Nine Divines") have abandoned us."*

:   **Belchimac:** *"We're doomed. The mine is going to stay closed, and we'll up*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *be carted of*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *to [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine") as slaves."*
:   **Enmon:** *"Only criminals get sent to Cidhna Mine. They're not going to send us there."*
:   **Belchimac:** *"Oh, they'll find some way to send us there. It'll be just my luck."*

:   **[Mena](/wiki/Skyrim:Mena "Skyrim:Mena"):** *"But why did they take her? What could they want with our little girl?"*
:   **Enmon:** *"I don't know. The guards are out looking for her, now. They'll be back soon."*
:   **Mena:** *"You keep saying that. What if she's gone forever? What if they've done something to her?"*

:   **Enmon:** *"Are you all right, dear?"*
:   **Mena:** *"The house is so... empty, Enmon... and quiet."*

:   **Enmon:** *"Are you all right, dear? I thought I saw a tear in your eye a moment ago."*
:   **Mena:** *"Oh, I'm fine, Enmon. I just... I still miss her."*
:   **Enmon:** *"I miss her, too, but I'm glad she's safe."*
:   **Mena:** *"So am I. I hope she's happy at the temple."*

:   **Mena:** *"Enmon, dear, do you have any regrets? About letting her go?"*
:   **Enmon:** *"No... no, we did the right thing. The temple will take good care of her, and one day she'll be helping all of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim")."*
:   **Mena:** *"You're right. She'll be a great Sybil, won't she?"*
:   **Enmon:** *"Of course she will. She's our daughter, after all."*

## Notes

- If you choose to allow Enmon to accompany you to the Forsworn camp, it is possible to command him like your regular follower by holding down the "talk" button at a slight distance from him.
  - By commanding Enmon to pick up items, you can outfit him with weapons and armor, making him a reasonably useful companion at lower levels. He will equip the best gear given to him upon changing cells.
  - Until you complete his related quest, Enmon will follow you indefinitely.

## Bugs

- After completing The Heart of Dibella, Enmon may behave as if he never met you upon returning to Karthwasten, returning to his default dialogue.

Ennis

**Ennis** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") who can be found at the [Cowflop Farmhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Cowflop_Farmhouse "Skyrim:Cowflop Farmhouse") in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). He shares his home with [Reldith](/wiki/Skyrim:Reldith "Skyrim:Reldith"), the [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") with whom he has lived since she rescued him after he was orphaned. His [prize goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gleda_the_Goat "Skyrim:Gleda the Goat") is stolen by you and sold to [a giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Grok "Skyrim:Grok") during the related quest.

He wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0001be1b "Skyrim:Clothing"), and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209aa "Skyrim:Clothing"). He carries an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Cowflop_Farm_Key "Skyrim:Cowflop Farm Key") to the farmhouse.

Ennis starts his day at 8am when he wakes up to work on his farm for twelve hours, ending his workday at 8pm. The only break from his work during the day is at 6:10pm, when he will take an hour to eat. Once he is finished with his work for the day, he will head inside his home to relax from the day's stresses. He will finally retire to his bed for the day at 11pm; waking up at 8am to start the next day.

## Related Quests

- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.

## Dialogue

His greetings can be:

:   *"Name's Ennis. If you've got friends who do business in Whiterun, they might know me."*
:   *"You talk to Reldith yet? She's like a mother to me."*
:   *"You here from the city? I visit Whiterun from time to time, mostly to make deals."*
:   *"Reldith is the hardest-working farmer in Rorikstead, but I'm the one with a head for business."*

### A Night To Remember

During A Night To Remember, he will be less friendly towards you. Should you approach him, he will force you into a conversation by saying:

:   *"You! You've got a lot of nerve showing yourself in this town again. What do you have to say for yourself?"*

You will be given two options in response:

:   **I'm sorry?**

    :   *"Sorry's not good enough! Not while my Gleda is still out there, alone and afraid. You kidnapped her and sold her to that Giant."*

:   **I have no idea what you're talking about.**

    :   *"Is that so? Does the name Gleda ring a bell? The star beauty of my farm? Kidnapped by a drunk lout and sold to a Giant? You'd better remember her right fast, before I call the guards and have you hauled away."*

Either option leads to:

:   **That sounds pretty bad...**
:   *"You're damned right it does. I'll never breed another prize-winning goat like Gleda! And don't you think of coming back to Rorikstead until you get her back from that Giant."*

You will then have a number of dialogue options, which will result in unique replies:

| Choice | Response |
| --- | --- |
| **What happened with Gleda again? I'm a little fuzzy on that.** | *You really don't remember stealing a goat and selling her to a Giant? Are you thick? Go get her! At least she's bound to follow you back - you smell just like the fermented feed she likes.* |
| **Did I say anything about where I left a [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose")?** | *You mentioned something like that... when you were running off with my goat! Tell you what - you bring back my goat, and maybe I'll give a damn about your staff.* |
| **Help me retrace my steps and I'll pay you for the goat.**  (*Bribe*: 1000 gold) | **Succeed**: *Fine, but I'll still be missing my Gleda. Doubt I'll ever have a prize winning goat again. Most of what you said was gibberish but you left a note. The only bit I could read was "after repaying [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") in Whiterun.* |
| **Fail**: *There's not enough money in the world to replace Gleda.* |
| **Tell me everything and you won't end up like your goat.**  (*Intimidate*) | **Succeed**: *Okay, okay. Most of what you said didn't make sense but you left a note. The only bit that I could read said "after repaying Ysolda in Whiterun." That's all I know.* |
| **Fail**: *Do what you have to do, I'm not giving up on Gleda.* |
| **I need to find [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne") and the staff, in order to get Gleda back.**  (*Persuade*) | **Succeed**: *I suppose that makes sense. You didn't mention a Sam and nothing you said about the staff made sense. You left a note but it was mostly gibberish, the only bit I could make out was "after repaying Ysolda in Whiterun.* |
| **Fail**: *You didn't seem to need either to sell Gleda to the Giant in the first place. I think you'll figure it out.* |

After returning the goat to Ennis, you can ask him for help in retracing your steps. With Gleda home, he will be grateful and freely offer some assistance:

:   *"Gleda! And not a scratch on her! Happy day! I still can't figure out why you stole her. You left a note explaining it, but half of it was gibberish and the rest had mead spilled on it. Only bit I could make out was "repaying Ysolda in Whiterun," and even that's mostly scribbles. Guess you could try there."*
:   **Now, what did I say about that staff?**
:   *"You said a whole lot of nonsense about selling Gleda to hire a priestess for some big event. There was a bit of talk about some staff you had in safe keeping. Never said where, but you sure didn't have it with you!"*

## Conversations

Ennis talking to Reldith

Ennis will often interact with the other residents of Rorikstead, particularly [Reldith](/wiki/Skyrim:Reldith "Skyrim:Reldith").

:   **Ennis**: *"Have you given my idea any more thought? You said you'd let me know yesterday, and that obviously didn't happen."*
:   **Reldith**: *"Oh, I don't know. Yes, we'd make more money, but I don't like the idea of you traveling alone out there with the [war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") and talk of [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon")."*
:   **Ennis**: *"Come on now, we discussed that. I wouldn't be traveling all of Skyrim. It'd just to Whiterun and back, that's it."*
:   **Reldith**: *"Tomorrow. I'll let you know tomorrow."*

:   **Reldith**: *"Another fine day at work in the fields. I don't envy those city folk who miss out on the joys of working the land."*
:   **Ennis**: *"I'll tell you who I don't envy - those poor children who lost their parents in this war."*
:   **Reldith**: *"Lives lost, crops burned, land ruined... there's no greater sin than war. And yet, you were an orphan, and you've made something of your life."*
:   **Ennis**: *"I was lucky. If you hadn't rescued me, I'd probably be a thief, a mercenary or something even worse."*
:   **Reldith**: *"It's too fine a day to dwell on such things. Let's get back to work and forget about wars and orphans for awhile."*

:   **Reldith**: *"The way our crops have been growing, Rorikstead must have the richest soil in the hold."*
:   **Ennis**: *"Maybe we should start selling the soil along with the dung. We could make a tidy profit."*
:   **Reldith**: *"Hah! Who in their right mind would pay for dirt? You'd get laughed out of Whiterun for even trying it."*
:   **Ennis**: *"Hey, people have paid money for stranger things. Take our cow dung - we sell that by the wagon load."*
:   **Reldith**: *"When you're rich, you can waste as much money as you like on far-fetched business ideas. In the meantime, there's a farm to run."*

Ennis will also discuss his business with [Jouane Manette](/wiki/Skyrim:Jouane_Manette "Skyrim:Jouane Manette").

:   **Jouane**: *"The last time I was in Whiterun, the tradesmen were talking about you. It seems your reputation as a businessman is growing."*
:   **Ennis**: *"Glad to hear all my hard work has paid off. Maybe we'll fetch a better price for our crops next time we're in the city."*

He will also converse with [Rorik](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik "Skyrim:Rorik") occasionally.

:   **Rorik**: *"I hear your crops sold well at the market. Well done, Ennis."*
:   **Ennis**: *"I'm trying something new, offering discounts for bulk purchases. So far, that seems to be working."*

If you ask Reldith where she sells her surplus crops, she'll mention Ennis in her response: *"In Whiterun, mostly. Ennis handles the business arrangements, but I know that he has a few purchasers who give us a fair price. Ennis prides himself on his shrewd business schemes. For my part, I'm far happier working with cattle and crops than with people."*

## Notes

- [Patch 1.5](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch#Version_1.5 "Skyrim:Patch") sets Ennis as essential. Although the patch notes the change as essential "until his part in A Night To Remember is completed", he is simply set as essential for the entirety of the game.

Ennoc inside Left Hand Mine

**Ennoc** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") who lives in the [Miner's Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Left Hand Miner's Barracks") for the [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine") in which he works.

Ennoc will spend all of his time mining, not ever breaking from his duties to eat or sleep. He wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"), and he carries a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Left_Hand_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Key to Left Hand Miner's Barracks") to the Barracks, and some [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

If you speak to Ennoc in Left Hand Mine, he will stay focused on his work, saying:

:   *"I'm just here to mine."*
:   *"Got ore to dig."*

Ennodius Papius

**Ennodius Papius**, an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial"), is a former [lumberjack](/wiki/Skyrim:Lumberjack "Skyrim:Lumberjack") now living an isolated existence in a small camp a short distance up the hill from his old workplace, [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill"). He is one of the first assigned targets after joining the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). He does not exist prior to the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius").

He wanders around all day long, at times sitting on a nearby rock, and, if the weather gets tough, warms his hands over the fire. At midnight he crawls into the tent for eight hours of sleep.

He wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261bd "Skyrim:Clothing"). He is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries a selection of [lower-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius")**: Kill Ennodius Papius.

### Kill Ennodius Papius

*"What? What do you mean? Oh! Oh... no... No!"*

When handing you the contract on Ennodius' head, [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") will provide a few facts about the target: *"He lives just outside Anga's Mill, in the woods. He was once the miller. Now Papius is just a paranoid recluse who thinks someone is out to get him. And he's right."* When you arrive at Anga's Mill, you may overhear a conversation between Ennodius' old colleagues, [Kodrir](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodrir "Skyrim:Kodrir") and [Leifur](/wiki/Skyrim:Leifur "Skyrim:Leifur"):

**Leifur**: *"Whatever happened to Ennodius? He just up and left."*
**Kodrir**: *"Don't know why you're asking me. But I'm glad that damn Imperial is gone. Something wrong about him."*
**Leifur**: *"You're all heart, Kodrir. I bet Lady Mara is weeping a special tear for you right now."*

When you approach the paranoid Imperial at his camp, he will be quite anxious, asking:

:   *"Why are you here? Get away from me!"*

Three options will be available:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| *"You were right to be paranoid, Ennodius."* | *"What? What do you mean? Oh! Oh... no... No!"* |
| *"Die, worm!"* | *"Aiiiiiiiieeeeee!"* |
| *(Remain silent)* | *"Who are you? You... you're with the Dark Brotherhood, ain'tcha? I knew it. I knew you'd come for me!"* |

All three options will make him flee with the words:

:   *"By the gods! Somebody help me!"*

## Notes

- Ennodius was supposed to be able to tell you a bit about himself if you met him outside the related quest. However, since he only spawns during the quest, this dialogue will never be heard: *"I used to work at Anga's Mill, but I... I had to leave."*, *"Someone's after me I tell you. They're watching me. Somewhere."* and *"Don't talk to me. You could be one of them."*
- Under the waterfall that is just upstream from Ennodius' camp, you can find three quicksilver ingots, a battleaxe, a barrel, a chest, and a strongbox (but see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Bugs

- The chest, quicksilver, and most of the battleaxe under the waterfall are placed beneath the surface, making them almost impossible to find unless your cursor is on exactly the right spot.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=18601))
